# 如何以「我原以为自己是女主……」为开头写一篇小故事？
- 点赞数：37915
- 更新时间：2022年08月24日16时31分26秒
- 回答url：https://www.zhihu.com/question/465978427/answer/1970969045
<body>
 <p data-pid="R_XRUXvL">【完结】千岁怎么了</p>
 <p data-pid="psPOfJYq">——</p>
 <p data-pid="59cFWMJf">我原以为自己是女主......</p>
 <p data-pid="QA63D0iI">直到...</p>
 <p data-pid="msGITxai">——</p>
 <p data-pid="7VsymgAD">我摸了摸平坦的胸口。</p>
 <p data-pid="Fn162aUI">——</p>
 <p data-pid="ueTIs9aX">哦，原来我是男主。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B9t5MkKD">站起来走两步。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V3LQ_cdK">不对劲！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1JN8g7nP">我转身，扒下裤子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TfXbMDam">哦，原来我是东方不败。</p>
 <p data-pid="2Si_xeu9">——</p>
 <h2>7月7</h2>
 <p data-pid="NTjCxQKo">——</p>
 <h3>好吧，我不是东方不败。</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DU8tqH-d">我就是个太监，呜呜呜。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gF0qZByF">嘤嘤嘤，人家还是想做回女孩子啦。</p>
 <p data-pid="Fb6SGHcj">——</p>
 <p data-pid="OKecjxFt">照镜子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="agIaGhz4">可恶，此等美貌，做太监也不是不行。</p>
 <p data-pid="BMSIZ6l5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4Zdeeus-">好在我是个有权有势的太监。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lpHUbGm0">嗯，可能还是个有点变态的太监。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uF-Ejr3V">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mguCqJy7">刚刚，看到自己太美，一时手抖，摔了镜子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x2jmKIy7">跪了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xV6u-9jJ">不是我跪了，是一堆人跪了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Sj7VnUY4">“千岁饶命！”</p>
 <p data-pid="ZHYnf8k9">“千岁饶命！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g-lw4ffA">这头磕得跟敲鼓似的，duangduang响。</p>
 <p data-pid="SZARy4TN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6_SQvbOx">批奏折。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="52U7aEEY">可恶，我有钱有权有美貌，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RqdHqIY_">为什么还要自己批奏折啊？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SPGz30on">越想越气。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MrBQbazk">把旁边穿黄袍的小东西领起来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d1cYytcf">对上他的卡姿兰大眼睛，我核善地微笑：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MaVmG7N-">“你是个成熟的小皇帝了，要学会自己批奏折。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v67MBXrW">小皇帝：？</p>
 <p data-pid="0hKCvI0D">义父今天好奇怪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lYv8vIIP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vV4t1Alj">脱衣服，浴桶泡澡。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nTGT5WV3">哇，我有马甲线哎，好棒。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VhYRfX0F">摸两下。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KoAmtWbc">流口水，马甲线竟然长我身上哎。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2J_DjBg6">有人掀帘子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8k3KaxkE">没忍住一掌打过去，人晕了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sMfW-d4l">仔细看，是美人晕了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KpJ61I4i">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NS__YU06">“来人啊！太医！宣太医！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P0Pq_jHA">电视剧都是这么叫的对吧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_AXgRwWl">太医来了，好帅。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Cg08_CnA">流口水。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r8GTZ94d">晕倒的美人也很美呢，愁，要哪个好呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t2jL80T0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VSErC89n">美人醒了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cqz3n4Kt">美人吐血了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nmOIlWYE">呜呜呜呜呜，病弱美人简直在我XP上疯狂蹦迪。</p>
 <p data-pid="ZTHZVjnQ">——</p>
 <p data-pid="ueFSHv8g">我道歉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o6waqJaF">“对不起，是我手快没忍住。”</p>
 <p data-pid="HcnfuVTe">这手它不受控制啊。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YeCCr_mf">——</p>
 <p data-pid="4aQYoAh9">美人挣扎着要下床。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XnicghaM">“容玦擅闯在先，甘愿受罚。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1i6_QmJD">——</p>
 <p data-pid="uvkFnP4U">美人叫容玦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nSnroSmQ">把容玦扶起来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pil6L4Sv">顺便摸了一下手。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8gVfNfgL">好滑。</p>
 <p data-pid="75IMX4HI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sEQxOKEI">容玦：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jCIkNMix">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fgplPEDW">美人养伤，挥泪告别。</p>
 <p data-pid="MIbBxNGA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JvPlX7nL">被参本子了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tpjgUoEK">“钱绥居心回测，竟然擅自调用御用太医！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HBOi4UPN">原来帅太医是御用的，难怪这么帅。</p>
 <p data-pid="CwFoBp61">等等，我叫钱绥？真省起名的功夫。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c_A72wTE">——</p>
 <p data-pid="Vyd8qR7g">话说不是我批奏折吗？我批我自己？</p>
 <p data-pid="4YCfaXBF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="etxyLfMQ">罚自己闭门思过三天。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lrFZs3s_">第一天，睡觉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EMRenEPc">第二天，睡觉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gCCFh-bQ">第三天，睡——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QvkfdQTe">睡不了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="donbD7Sz">被小皇帝找上门了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Igv4rgSc">——</p>
 <p data-pid="do3oRxH_">“义父——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7LOTsZkV">明黄色的炮弹撞进我怀里。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jXrjAYlh">救命，我的胸肌好痛。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rz3X-Rdj">“阿宣好想义父。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UY-dVpdN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9AWrg0oV">脸上被蹭了一嘴口水。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w30vpnwx">生气气。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gnlTYJ48">领小皇帝起来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C-KUcSXc">“爸爸没你这个好大儿。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NAyUETfR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m78Zwaxk">小皇帝哭了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5ECxZC58">下人跪了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jjc9Kzic">——</p>
 <p data-pid="6sPRlqzh">好吧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HuE0H1o4">抱小皇帝，亲一口。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y8nM2TGS">“爸爸最喜欢你这个好大儿了。”</p>
 <p data-pid="8L5tywAw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CuZhY82r">小皇帝懵了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kVoDp_py">下人跪得像伏地魔。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4avySPQG">——</p>
 <p data-pid="-u3H6rg6">你们好难伺候哦。</p>
 <p data-pid="n6BOPKsW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iUmMIntE">闭门思过结束了，回去上班。</p>
 <p data-pid="2xt452KH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V_ZLflGL">批奏折。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3PeSE8yE">批奏折。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Zlducs2I">批奏折。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="igk_EEbO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gJNDrZde">想放假，想看美人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jMY761eM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n-R5AS3n">去看容玦，带了礼物。</p>
 <p data-pid="_jwp52Q-">——</p>
 <h2>7月8</h2>
 <p data-pid="TgW_Mz10">——</p>
 <h3>容玦在看书。</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PpybO7cl">妈妈，他好好看。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t4j0zSHS">不行，我得想办法娶了这个男人。</p>
 <p data-pid="7m1Q_z2O">——</p>
 <p data-pid="B6erq0vt">开玩笑的。</p>
 <p data-pid="g0IO2JJG">——</p>
 <p data-pid="O12nzdjI">容玦打开礼物。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UQdjLqVB">——</p>
 <p data-pid="zgq2wsl8">“喜不喜欢？”</p>
 <p data-pid="NyAGCjQk">我专门找帅太医要的大补品。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LemGHcrT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OSVa5xz2">？</p>
 <p data-pid="PrV3LEFo">救命，帅太医怎么给我准备了牛鞭鹿茸？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TQqZ1bUo">——</p>
 <p data-pid="H3jXWIir">容玦脸黑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8ktvUV3U">——</p>
 <p data-pid="NGYIyGNk">不行，我得圆回来。</p>
 <p data-pid="lmuFhhco">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BCJGZsOF">在容玦的注视下，我匆匆盖上盒子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g3_IBRtE">“哈，说出来你可能不信。其实这个......是我准备自己吃的。最近有点虚。那个......一不小心拿错了......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H8URjhRb">——</p>
 <p data-pid="ii9OSbHp">看我闪闪的水灵灵大眼睛。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PQPkmgWY">他肯定信了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lBhcbC81">——</p>
 <p data-pid="a6T889U8">好吧，他不信。</p>
 <p data-pid="pKO6aQoY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aODdIyiN">唉，可能惹美人生气了。愁。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4jTFwNWW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6kNHyhcM">当权臣好难。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vHs5tu52">不想批奏折。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b1f4JSoY">——</p>
 <p data-pid="OamBsNJX">又被参本子了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3w48aGv_">“钱绥区区宦官，屋舍极尽奢华，养男宠三千......骄奢淫逸，仗势欺人......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GDQl82hD">——</p>
 <p data-pid="IOxUE0hA">？</p>
 <p data-pid="lZzUr91j">男宠？</p>
 <p data-pid="5rBZFMsB">在哪？</p>
 <p data-pid="1ULbwlmZ">我男宠呢？</p>
 <p data-pid="xYpjuRzD">——</p>
 <p data-pid="qxx0ptQL">问下人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tpgz5EhP">下人抖得像在筛糠。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2ngn9lF8">“大人，这、容公子......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FgS51Sjz">——</p>
 <p data-pid="VPrgMH-A">！？</p>
 <p data-pid="cC3ri0MD">美人竟是我老婆？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AhqWO9Eo">——</p>
 <p data-pid="MxGsdb0h">老婆生气了，怎么办，愁。</p>
 <p data-pid="Il6mMhEs">——</p>
 <p data-pid="z4aEUTvI">找个人问问。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3TS6W3qV">——</p>
 <p data-pid="EayswkzH">捏小皇帝的脸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P6ZS-SBu">“陛下，我惹我老婆生气了。该咋办？要不你赏点东西给我去哄老婆？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tbclr_5y">“老婆是谁？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fKNRZZeC">“这个嘛...这你问住我了。可能是后半生会一直陪你在一起的人？啊不对不对，我说的老婆是指美人。”</p>
 <p data-pid="csuELAuY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MU9VAzVA">小皇帝眼睛亮了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GOltgrjR">“义父当阿宣老婆可好？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XCbMTdXt">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v9QBSXK2">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lINEwIjr">“这应该不太行。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e1eIi3Zh">没满十四周岁，犯法。</p>
 <p data-pid="AzLJOTb5">——</p>
 <p data-pid="9Bjvm730">小皇帝瘪嘴。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QgtQ2klJ">小皇帝哭了。</p>
 <p data-pid="B_AbF_Q9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QlcXbhA1">救命，不要哭了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kKUfZx_B">整得我好像欺负小孩的变态。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m8qCqm2a">——</p>
 <h2>7月9</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>坏了，哄不好了。</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tMjVBYDQ">要不打晕算了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wdvzy7gq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WpwVDapB">算了，犯法。</p>
 <p data-pid="PEtz2LL7">——</p>
 <p data-pid="DpbKy6ZY">有人喊：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="33AfgvDQ">“见过太傅——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wa62_nGF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lm7koEFx">小皇帝顿时不哭了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z378w-Gz">甚至打了个嗝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xFR5Komu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6qztsRWg">话说，太傅是皇帝老师对吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t7vjL-C6">咋这么年轻？</p>
 <p data-pid="J6nVSzBx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UECt8037">哇，又是一个美人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1oODn4dn">冷峻美人我也可以的！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Bqu4FPkX">我不挑！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FcxRvab3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vTpKUu64">小皇帝被太傅训了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-gcrU6RJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Atfy6oQi">好像委屈巴巴的折耳猫，哈哈哈哈哈哈哈。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zYphZ-bN">你也有今天。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xMufFXhk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1rQwrX6e">可能笑太大声了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D5hfMKLc">太傅瞥了我一眼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dSjJcogw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bJA8UNsK">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TVgICuc0">他是不是冲我翻白眼？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3sgpc7uC">我警告你，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5nu0ziY3">我就没有见过</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cHT8NdkM">翻白眼这么好看的人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nOM6SvkI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hJFurJ83">算了，溜了吧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tf51-bKA">围观骂孩子不太好。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J8r8nxI6">——</p>
 <p data-pid="gs2JqZ7q">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B9yiwEqI">怎么走不动？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rzw2ZW3Z">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="34LYpwng">小折耳猫，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="auYZb9pd">我告诉你，扯我衣角也没用。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HLxtz681">你爹我不会帮你求情的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d0ouZC-k">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="84Q9HtxG">“太傅莫怪，陛下年纪尚轻，方才摔了一跤，疼痛难忍才会哭闹......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q4PEeGmO">哼，罢了，帮帮这小兔崽子。</p>
 <p data-pid="SlcaEmY0">好歹是我弄哭的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YxukmTQN">——</p>
 <p data-pid="DL_s9Pr-">太傅好高冷，好帅。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R21y-M-A">连扯嘴角的弧度都那么完美。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ED0e9arI">“陛下龙体要紧，既摔了一跤，何不宣太医？来人，去太医院找赵太医。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZqBvDvgo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K-YGqlbj">不是吧，这也要找太医？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5nt6llZn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pZUaa0pS">哈，还是熟人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P9_O9Fab">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B-kPbjFR">招手手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wWRIovuX">帅太医好久不见！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x95UThcR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O46UGNAV">嘤嘤嘤，赵太医干嘛不理人家。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WQggsOup">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NXNKsUXD">怎么回事？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p2LzDEHQ">太傅看我的眼神好像在看傻子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dZqk8skC">——</p>
 <h2>7月10</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>太傅让赵太医给小皇帝看病。</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Lk0Kg2eF">小皇帝躲我身后了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kjcAwaKN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AY1ZxSaC">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zX0t0tSb">好吧，我摊牌。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ya5vg41q">他没事。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AoHJq-wS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nMCr-7xl">我摊牌了，我装的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tp25z0jq">笑话，摊什么牌。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ugjV2ofA">我堂堂糊弄学大师没见过这种小场面？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="urIDjnIV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dy8cel5T">我转身就是</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qRw5Jx_L">一个弱柳扶风</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qKhx0m2E">倒在太医身上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hY5N7DlH">“赵太医，人家好像不太舒服。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YT8AjcW_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LW7a7HGB">赵太医身上好冷，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jTcrnKg3">夏天贴贴一定很舒服吧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2nMdZ6Bt">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zk777zxS">赵太医怎么不做声？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="emG6AcKQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xaenrR_n">不对劲，气氛不对劲。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TlepKd76">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n2L6SVA5">悄咪咪抬头看一眼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W9gFAXV4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lch1btc1">危！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IP-ZeI4h">靠错人了！是太傅！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NpGHN_Fr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gEXQesvA">冷静，我不尴尬，尴尬的就是别人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XKO-Iki1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OzVET_Z1">给太傅披件衣服。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qXzbSrKD">“太傅身上有点凉，多穿点。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_ww8f9B9">要不让赵太医给您瞧瞧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LLVHke0X">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o553xw2Z">！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Dg-Be4pM">好像感觉更冷了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gi3UeJ9s">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y62_8WQB">“突然想起来府里的灶台还烧着我先走了后会有期。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QckPTbMr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fp-Pspwh">溜了溜了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i1yzDNNo">对不住了小皇帝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tkxhXA0Q">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FuW1M9oz">第二天。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M_rLH4nz">上班，批奏折。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TX_g1x-U">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UARWRJro">小皇帝跑来诉苦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3VWe5lZi">说被太傅罚抄礼记。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BqlY3Kx5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QsGnm-6y">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9hgvUhbz">不要这样看我，再看我也不可能帮你抄的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dy1eLG27">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EGeFLIV8">认命，抄一半吧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rBSoieP6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5GfnsYYI">写字太丑被小皇帝嫌弃，他决定自己抄了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UCMiTJ1I">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="456SXjRk">我怒了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QS2x95uU">小东西，你怎么敢的？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3EBM0-3t">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p4x91Fbm">我报复心很强的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N9VM4CFh">我要摧毁他心中的光！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZmfIRjJW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cqtUuFBn">“陛下，或许，你知道奥特曼吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g-deH4Sc">——</p>
 <p data-pid="eBGPoBtr">小皇帝：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6ng00ew0">“那是什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HkNeUrck">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dV2CzkHx">我笑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P9y6Hutj">给小皇帝讲了奥特曼的全集故事。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FsqbOsR4">甚至生动形象地亲自表演。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xAHT4-GV">迪加光波！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fUP6hrIo">( o|o)ノ三三三三三三三三三</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YDVIm1TB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qLqHtU4a">很好，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ij_6Hj3p">皇帝坚信不疑</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OltUo5al">奥特曼是正义的化身，是世界的光。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2F972H4g">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O0CpmL6q">时机到了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gmxKpWPz">我轻轻凑近他耳边，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c1yX4Ep8">犹如恶魔低语：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vNukhX4G">“我骗你的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fkrDkexc">奥特曼，是假的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="miVbwbSM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XnJXgOEk">小皇帝瞪眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RqtAJRqm">小皇帝震惊，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U13Do4lC">小皇帝瘪嘴。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GSnLcVx6">“哇——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5nTkiFN7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9qDSVIWP">糟糕，玩大发了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qK3XNZct">他哭太大声了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PGANb4Ii">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1Z3M6lpA">要不我还是跑吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Iq0TYYUW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aZqEIVf4">等等，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DpO15aiQ">我看见了谁？！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="glanUbgl">太傅你站门口多久了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月11</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>完了，他肯定看见我刚刚打怪兽的英勇身姿了。</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MV1Lyli7">该死，我就知道，没人能拒绝奥特曼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0KaqY_cA">可惜了，你的偶像终究是空。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cX-6cwYu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tE33Gxrd">我怜悯地看他一眼，拍拍他肩膀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jn8XKCHQ">“太傅，节哀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fo7had4f">偶像千千万，不行咱就换。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Lj2GyivU">或许，你知道铠甲勇士吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2IUfhJ4a">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XuSjZx0I">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R73HXCz7">怎么又开始制冷了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RvCvPetd">太傅是不是看谁都像傻逼？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oZ4rnBRy">不然为啥他每次都这样看我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RuGE8GHL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UqGuAY-b">身后传来小皇帝声音：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VSVMvy0v">“义父——，哇......嗝......哇......嗝......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8JNmKnyl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rl_2r-0U">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dAGBLnvP">“太傅，我要先走了，回见。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BeMbLKGO">再不走，我怕走不了了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wu9Hzywu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EQueRK1k">小皇帝又落在太傅手里了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8lVNUiI5">我实在有点愧疚。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GbWMxaGr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TO0__wop">哎，明天给他讲讲铠甲勇士吧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="26xVQPJ3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dIgxYEnu">好久没见到容玦美人了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VHlEtoyL">不知道他伤好了没有。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Eft0L6AU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CGltqkbK">带礼物看容玦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2p5i4KsY">这次是人参。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3FoNu3xw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B_VDaBh4">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7R6zDMPo">美人旁边的红衣美人是谁？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KONaiGoA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iZ_r4IxD">不是，你们美人都是扎堆的吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sI23RxET">不要钱呀</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LvdT0GIm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aNbmViAN">两个美人对我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2VbRx0iq">“见过千岁。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2EvIxoQi">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jvhv-m7N">我左手一个右手一个，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Sd-qhh1M">扶起来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yBFJLs60">摸一把手。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-WaCSOoW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NVCAYzPs">红衣美人的手有点糙啊。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1niRrXnR">要多涂点护手霜。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4LGgdz1U">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LITjZlG8">红衣美人一把甩开我的手。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r_tgVxdg">凤眼喷火，柳眉倒竖。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g9DEQlLe">“钱大人请自重。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tp3cyLYa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q78s7msz">世间竟有如此清纯不做作的男子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SiTkeWXK">男人，你成功引起了我的注意。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MWltguGJ">“你叫什么名字？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WD_cv8_C">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fSHqXQQe">容玦淡淡扫我一眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n7OF4w09">“大人忘了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3OVWaTD1">他是，季晏。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QApI38Ei">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mhdcAj3P">我掏掏耳朵，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="85SY1WI3">啥？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hwEt6um8">鸡眼？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LkRw02Rz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uaohw6FJ">怜悯地看一眼红衣美人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D9mPbXvH">咋就起了这样的名字。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6nEl__Xj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bQp3rcX-">容玦看上去恢复得不错，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OPnSH5Bg">也接受了我带的人参。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BHyaprjV">他一定不生我气了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1bbRxiGD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mp3Q7FNx">既然这样......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wfF4YTvk">要不......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ol1CdiS8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VonFpjj0">“容玦，那个，今晚我能歇你这不？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z925TPVc">看我扑闪扑闪的大眼睛，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3r8jmJd3">不可能有人忍心拒绝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OJioOhIr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0bQ6mNa8">嘤嘤嘤，容玦拒绝了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bWEqjOjH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1jEv1vmW">不，我不信。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SBePzQWl">他心里有我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9_sAFvyh">哼，男人，你又在玩欲擒故纵的小把戏。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FTC63Jir">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4z4WgFaS">“容玦身体尚未恢复，不如大人今晚去季晏处歇息？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WtFPh3t0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a5k5AnNp">唉？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5u5UYaKT">季晏，</p>
 <p data-pid="AKCFscf-">你怎么回事？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6NOwtK9p">我知道我的魅力很大的啦，但是我们才第一次见面......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uVH5vSCb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SqmxbN4G">最后稀里糊涂地去了季晏屋里。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gj9j_0XW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yUFxaifG">话说我不是有男宠三千吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S7E7TSAc">咋就看见俩？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Mfsz-RAr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vj6yQ4pg">不重要啦，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UDgcpBFN">美人不在多，好看就行。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8J-ns4em">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ptemrrth">季晏屋里挂了一排亮蹭蹭的刀和剑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cHqTEqC1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7T5ZTYZO">季晏摸了一下其中的一把刀</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zlRaSW1t">回头冲我笑：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FWhg5ifr">“大人，请。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gieIRMn8">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="45cfFDQA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BIZcWG3h">季晏说要和我喝酒。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oR0lPmzU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9zBbVO2F">说到这个，我就不困了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mHaPIv3S">呵，喝酒，我没怕过谁。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FFnBEww2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RSFwlGfL">我拿起酒坛就是一口，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="62W2_HcQ">一脚踏凳子上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YrWIr-vz">“真男人就上坛子。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mvSyjY-k">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BsIl9GAk">听了我这话，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ezO7jJ43">季晏面色古怪地看了一眼我的脸，眼神逐渐往下。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DW6RhC5M">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m1vCCAoZ">哎哎哎，你看哪呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PtPPfiKC">我不要面子的啊？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lxfljQn8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bYyFgCcy">喝酒。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-R3Zjy7d">你一杯，我一杯。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0iT2r2aR">你一杯，我一杯。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sUGHpDZr">你一杯，我一杯。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JIWmQDee">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lrOO2MDA">就这？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fwe-_RQ9">打发谁啊？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eopydjfs">上坛子！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ld_hw--8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fZFEHCBl">“两只小蜜蜂啊——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VPA_qxYg">飞在花丛中啊——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qIEMuiDw">飞呀——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZW7eQqF5">嘿！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QwvH-5bS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U35xKhnQ">“你、你输了，喝！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="do24WTmp">我摇摇晃晃地把坛子砸桌子上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N3-eiE8C">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sXXG6i1Y">季晏面色酡红，握紧拳头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mMYKHQ-b">一把端起酒坛。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rpkdJGq0">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mBPV6u9j">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hk5iZGwt">妈耶，好多美人</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4OLs484c">好多、多红衣服美人</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mMDd5cvn">就是看起来好像站不太稳，有点晃悠</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2wDNBht0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sZ36xsVt">早上感觉呼吸不畅，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k4k07wW2">睁眼，在季晏床上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-EjzonOi">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="24-OqenB">季晏像个八爪鱼一样缠我身上，手臂差点勒死我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VJVPIebp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mZkOcRp7">昨晚喝断片了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Lksxr-IB">妈妈，我忘记我不是我了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jp1dM6Yv">呜呜呜，我再也不是千杯不醉了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mO3tviiR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gb9_53v3">季晏醒了，一把推开我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WbCY4C_3">他手忙脚乱地整理衣服，庆幸地发现自己贞洁还在。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I5hZT_NN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BqNm1FeW">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vYRSxyzo">男人，是我给你的自由过了火。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月12</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>大早上的，我衣衫不整的被季晏赶出来。</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p8LkREH2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R3zMWROb">季晏砰一声关了门。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gv8-YFql">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m6L31x8h">淦，差点撞到我英俊的鼻子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pHXgqwjY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ji4ywKx1">回到自己屋子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B3KH1gkT">有侍从问我要不要赏季晏。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_PWoreJw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jmOsBgMn">赏？赏啥？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CmfMfHZy">我摸摸下巴。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-BU01ndT">好像懂了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YRuizKCG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NJ_aHeEq">吩咐人去赵太医那要了些质地滑腻的香膏。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UwO8uFwA">派人送去给季晏。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="spCfK24e">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yW6kYEi0">上班，批奏折。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1P8aWa7R">讲铠甲勇士，哄小皇帝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jTBU4p0-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mSrMyYJC">下班，回府。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v-ApK6Yq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SX1AzfDR">嗯？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2rql-58q">听说季晏收到香膏后大发雷霆，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="F_GGbvPH">当场捏爆了香膏盒，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="55q31WG4">并且提刀砍了院子里的三棵树。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q1EsXJ26">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7AxrGS4R">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vBIi0b3p">真奇怪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KjA90vjR">找容玦问问。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="36lfZaF-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W9KF6Q3X">容玦见我来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="16H3iAH3">难得的眼中流露出三分惊讶三分惊喜两分幽怨一分哀愁。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x-zRaeZP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KTPhg3TJ">你问我还有一分是什么？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K6T3g5hL">当然是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jyrCoCdi">因为我编不出来了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oSyaX6tq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cV8ptEnE">“容玦，你说季晏干嘛发这么大脾气？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZxBIUZ1B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aDfygZpU">怀疑容玦被太傅夺舍了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fifik0w1">看我的眼神跟太傅看我一模一样。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-T3wvHd8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qXngfG7V">容玦端起茶杯，缓缓开口：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="43xEfp_p">“听闻大人送了礼物给季晏。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QaIRC6Cv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XuV67ri3">“是呀，香膏呀。不喜欢也不用这么生气吧。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pltsZvle">摊手，美人的心思真难懂。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ftr6fTtD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ou35mjAl">“我问赵太医要了很多呢。要不剩下的给你？反正季晏也不喜——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VFMp9qZx">咳咳咳——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OAjD_ksx">容玦被茶呛到了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_B_RsFRt">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xUdCmOOB">容玦咳红了脸，说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NlFGOdNr">“我不要！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZhREwmtR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="79cl0W71">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hi23edet">不太懂，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DfnKu3R2">护手霜而已，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_nDGyYKL">为什么美人们都不喜欢？</p>
 <p data-pid="YtVudB9k">——</p>
 <h2>7月13</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>最后，一个香膏都没送出去。</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NG0ZpTna">算了，拿来自己擦手手擦jiojio。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i4A4P3_K">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RPXEPN40">对了，既然季晏被气到砍树，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-l7xDaxk">那我只有...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pfYJDE40">罚他再种回来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="khPtcBdL">保护环境，人人有责。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H_GE610G">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TN7d3esL">侍从去通知季晏种树，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7nS8i1D-">回来说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jgSHhrYZ">季晏又大发雷霆，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jpmCF2ya">把院墙砸了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UI3pwHI5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fm6aNHpR">我怒了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="omUB6Pp0">这我能忍？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FqBjTJqx">搁这拆家呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8-gkPbat">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eeYvZDrC">我：“让他把院墙补上。告诉季晏，如果不补，我就天天去他院子里歇息！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="34QrPBbx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rbt0BjgS">又是新的一天。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yoqQem-L">早起，打哈欠，准备上班。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Kbrvdq3U">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iuDJ0vgs">嗯？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VSHViw61">侍从说今天休沐？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BEc2mydd">好耶！不用上班！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IGsjx04D">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dgmefgoA">决定偷偷出去玩。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pWbXX5tR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SIJ5GLGI">换好衣服，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gSH5TxqP">在镜子前臭美。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7fUyz8al">噢，魔镜魔镜，我是不是最美的人？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aB1rZft1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="60uGJCX-">臭美完了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hy410vZQ">瞥一眼侍从。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IiOsMEKz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Is0tilYh">我还没开口，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N43HOhGG">侍从一副秒懂的样子：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AZrEEC0s">“大人放心！属下绝不泄露一个字！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0KDUiWHs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A7mx52tA">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P_724LoG">你懂个锤子哦，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NvDWl5Qt">我是叫你去拿点钱给我，没钱玩个毛线。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7jj1zBTZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3CxlKUoL">出门前，拿把折扇耍耍帅。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7kssDUeo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RgU1E0mS">都到古代了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="82OI_1IF">能不去打卡青楼？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RORHIOZ2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kzpVseRM">不知道青楼的姑娘小倌有没有我好看。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="COLCzGE7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SiKmUFl-">怕人认出来，特地找了个偏一点的青楼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="upGW7Z7I">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AHRiG0dg">美人们，我来了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cqM30-Py">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4sXr-7vi">点了花魁。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8bSw4rgA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-CtAepE-">笑死，一个怎么够？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tMrS6r-p">老鸨，来十个最漂亮的美人！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EccWBzNq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1DcKbO6o">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ACLAc8ex">送进来的怎么有男有女？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-rERnFo5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GoicpfQi">好像也没毛病。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a_XIIL-_">算啦，不重要啦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V65YCNIU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K_b04uqB">听琵琶，喝美酒，品美食，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FoBLTtyK">美人在怀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XiqQQq1K">就一个字，爽！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3bnUOteR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SCm6FyG0">喝了好几坛酒，醉意上头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bm2SSKd6">我料想我的脸应该很红了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="18ziB3X5">躺在花魁的怀里，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8XmY3GvL">微微闭上眼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i1VmMOS3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Msk8TWl8">“大人？大人？奴家今晚服侍大人好不好？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XcIt3L3l">花魁的柔荑抚摸上我的脸，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xUi5NKKx">娇柔的唇瓣似乎碰了一下我的耳垂。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tw0hLElF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i-klpOeW">我的意识朦朦胧胧，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2gRSIYTg">只捕捉到关键词，今晚？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XlwEh1tU">今晚干啥？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ocleEN7v">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0CIhqusT">干啥都不行，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4-bc5D2P">我还有好些奏折没批呢。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oZQMzaYp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U2r7Dgd3">醉花楼的花魁从未见过这样的客人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q9TC1Y2c">他一身素衣，面容俊美非凡。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2fozphre">一口气叫了十个姑娘小倌，却只是饮酒听乐，不做其他 。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vykW-oqL">此时，他面色桃红，嘴唇微张，微微颤动着似沾有泪的长睫。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TExWpMpv">他躺在自己怀里，简直——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iAGZMfOi">简直比自己还像个花魁。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kY0fTJCX">旁边的一个小倌不安分的要摸上他的腰，被她冷冷扫了一眼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BxMqw6VM">小倌悻悻收回了手。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K1iiKmpk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OSy5OB2Q">花魁一向自恃清高，不愿委身于人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fj-BAnLW">但如果是他......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TfdxtZJ5">于是她凑近了他耳边喃喃细语......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2NssehcC">他有些醉了，她附耳过去才听见他的回答。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J4F4NEgc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="woEwRuK_">我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i6pz-8hk">“啥今晚......啥都不行！我要回去......批......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zgiDp6CJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iCGT61NJ">这醉花楼的酒真是好、好啊好</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ljtds69E">美、美人也不、错</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VlkgeX5J">好评！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6B3W9tXm">下、下次再来！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Duksajmw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ituVbO39">失去意识前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oVWDKdjo">我感到腰上一松，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W3MpcsiW">然后听见砰的一声，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xJ6nPpAy">门倒了？</p>
 <p data-pid="64nAKTSS">——</p>
 <h2>7月14</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>砸门声让我酒醒了大半。</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oHmjHzi-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wButpb-t">我一个垂死病中惊坐起，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IjJIcM3i">揽着花魁一个侧翻，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="REv4z027">滚到旁边。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CN6FyQ7w">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T865jKGJ">好险好险，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q9lHomUy">差点被被门压了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uHe9GTKq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EucnF6ec">什么情况？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WUqO3fd2">我，钱绥，逛青楼</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4shik-QQ">居然被砸场子了？！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dJSxqyI4">这说出来你敢信？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C_m75wvX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CKO7pcDS">我从花魁身上爬起来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aNUQeK0M">爷倒要看看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aAuWdje1">哪个崽种敢惹到我头上？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BdGayS0-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K229wP4b">我看向门外。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q2KxvK2O">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xZiDqdaH">嗯？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NSR5VSVR">“季晏？太傅？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wjbZY75f">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TMInBUgK">一定是我眼花了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wW7ET_cn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jYvvoCRH">把倒在地上的门强行堵回去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4PjXwYli">再躺回花魁怀里。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ljDRN_MU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pMnKXdOu">我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l8cbrW10">“继续...奏乐...”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2OVWJe5e">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OkBXwMBN">姑娘小倌们面面相觑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ykRC4q6T">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R9fKyAEa">门外传来季晏的怒吼：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ecBmunoa">“钱！绥！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D8EOuKu4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2o7jydp6">救命！我没眼花！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tEXCWn6r">他们俩怎么在这！？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bNrdsnZA">又不是捉奸！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dNRXCv56">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BML8PzFS">我一个鲤鱼打挺，夺门而出。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yp8_3jUb">从此醉花楼少了一扇门。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SwGJSyoa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="58XKCaQK">“还敢跑？！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PF76ukwi">季晏火冒三丈地追上来了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-u7hcEox">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xSweEQWx">他一手抓住了我的袖子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ofu-DeR5">我条件反射转身回击。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cbHhB-Nc">嗬——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Mke1Vfhl">你一招，我一招</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gfSRiqgn">你一招，我一招</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XctoIYxk">你一招，我一招</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2l5hgZXZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_UDqXRU7">达咩！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gwQRd5Sg">再打我衣服要掉光了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q9D_5fHZ">本来就没穿牢。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NB30hHck">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q2xYlo9m">季晏也停了手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Kx8tRCif">而且很诡异地脸红了，侧过脸去不看我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T6yM2a0W">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u9QEBZ8Q">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v8eqdkia">你脸红个茶壶泡泡？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AsOg0Iry">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jTcwkcQe">季晏说：“你跑什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i0NinfNg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DNYT1NNf">“你不追我跑什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YMmzxYJb">“你不跑我追什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="asUqvmBo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GvBugt16">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w3zZVu8h">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FEECn8nZ">季晏不知道哪搞来一披风，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3h759wk3">直接罩我身上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YuqyRmy7">还说我不成体统？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="weQtlfBZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W0p_IVwD">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fqqJ7PiI">到底谁是男宠？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hcc2sEy6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FvXnb_F6">好吧，最后还跟季晏回府了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iB9mnB7Z">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="61nApJDO">突然，我发现了盲点。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YlcyLirr">季晏...好像是和太傅一起出现的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A4SLQW6y">太傅也去逛青楼了？！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0l7vReCr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XG0mytDp">好像也没什么哦，毕竟我都能去了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="If_QHqTY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SKnYJ5Gk">管它呢，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T_xxrFTb">累了，回府倒头就睡。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oXryrSgD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g7axh000">只是没想到啊，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MtQb9ga9">很快啊，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="seSWhU6c">京城里就传遍了我的风流轶事。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6APYmu53">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Dq3K1vBD">“听说钱绥逛醉花楼被男宠抓回去了！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Os4eKv3i">“不是，是钱绥和男宠逛醉花楼，两人为花魁大打出手！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mb3Vr1Mn">“非也非也！是钱绥为争花魁名号暴打了醉花楼的姑娘！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hT_2Gl8Y">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i-9TwDZ2">“钱绥去醉花楼当花魁了！”</p>
 <p data-pid="mO5xEOGY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月15</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>？</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sRyXJufV">不是，这谣言都有人信？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="btcxfGqs">我：地铁，老人，手机.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lvH6Oa5n">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5kM6hcZh">小小的脑袋，大大的疑惑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QSn3fo-4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JRpLV54v">我问侍从：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DvQ815_q">“你觉得我能干出这种事？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wRtaxVps">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5Jnwl0-Y">侍从：...紧张</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RcqbyJi1">“......不能......吧……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6sYlUoHv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pdgkf3Y7">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MZAS10EB">能不能把吧字去掉？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HXZAS0xL">你是不是犹豫了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k0nFdgJd">生气气。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O5MfZqLC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VCHi3X2m">照常上班，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5EqvO8fO">批奏折。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N9G4s0Bh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7JFL9xVh">小皇帝扯我袖子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ol4Udrdu">看他一眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NFj-ptst">“干啥？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BFDJKTLf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EXIzjeC4">“义父，花魁是什么？义父为什么要当花魁？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G4GIf3My">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-8lV2UTy">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DTIEnIAh">哪个崽子教他的？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nfKdeOk9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s2_uBYkO">我拍拍他毛茸茸的头，说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KxyoIfil">“花魁，就是花中魁首。说别人是花魁就是夸他好看的意思。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XaQ3g0j7">我说的完全没问题吧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h1Bl8ieg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7J099LT5">小皇帝瞪大眼睛，似有所悟。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5kFwu6VG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fUXEkBsd">第二天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b5FxP7rp">听说小皇帝被罚抄十遍论语。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yQE20o_W">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zHCKBy8J">起因是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-5TSQhVQ">他夸太傅像个花魁。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LcI6D3TX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-GCqyuhF">噗</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6MBiwY9g">哈哈哈哈哈哈哈哈</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7UOfKlYP">太傅啊太傅，你也有今天</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8vgFR3OG">——</p>
 <p data-pid="JvspeR1t">......</p>
 <p data-pid="P5m-BEvC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6rHfilAM">救命，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sDIRutMq">最近三伏天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eBE1xdAd">我要热融了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SIunafoP">冰块已经不能满足我了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6SS4DGUO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YWNU7q7d">然而，聪明绝顶的我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hVBu1fWT">想起来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BSosIPQy">太傅会制冷！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n5krcpyp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V-UM4Yms">“太傅，不要走！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VflGOzlp">上完早朝后，我及时拦住了太傅。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oRu_qLj1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dN-3630T">太傅转身，皱眉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4ELNXGDs">很好，冷气技能开始释放了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6u7zLUrU">得想个法子加强技能。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eMUKh8qg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P6u8P89S">有了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rl3NpGhT">“太傅，人家好像中暑了~”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O1iSiXy5">我使出一招特技，弱柳扶风，倒在太傅怀里。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ruDpTZqv">果然，好凉快~</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-HtSb_KC">这冰冰的腹肌谁不爱？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lt8g4zOJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Iv_LiWvs">糟糕，太傅使出一招凌波微步，瞬间转移了位置。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LZorLWPi">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_Bq64-Q6">我使出一个狗皮膏药技能，又贴了上去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dU34pgh7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6V__GDr5">太傅：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dvY78BG1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月16</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>我被太傅揍了一顿，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R_TaaicH">这说出来可能没人信。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EKv7PXCm">毕竟，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BjlAs7uz">我，钱绥，武力值max</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M9vsSD4O">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S6WwJAu8">哎，谁让太傅的猫猫拳如此可爱？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4oMx_Tl8">让人心甘情愿挨打。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SvYPt4iP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XVstVh13">而且，挨打附送的冷气体验实在令我着迷。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x7bUe35B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zZ87q0G2">又一天下早朝后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3mYtr5Bz">我四处寻找太傅身影。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m-3BiM05">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6dUGjUT1">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ti3nh54R">人呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Qpcek6zv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XOf_e-hd">随机抽取了个下朝的幸运官员，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Vy_t4WGH">我：“看见太傅没有？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GVHq0IVf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p1OyF6eR">官员：T_T</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2_tTdEwB">“太、太傅最近告病休假了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tRKTmicl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kFP7K-ek">可恶，竟然让他逃了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v3eOrcWs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="llhgYXwj">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iLUHAtRp">热，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V2SLMDgS">心烦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RjTe5Mky">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aQR5Dc4k">找容玦聊天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gJQaHRO2">问他为什么穿那么厚一点都不热？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R-Sejy4S">他告诉我心静则凉，并且建议我下围棋？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3ARja874">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6pnm7MA7">我嘲讽一笑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c0T1-jOo">愚昧的唯心主义者啊！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fTCZTSeK">你知道你面对的是一个学过《哲学生活》的人吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JOS4rZei">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U_ZIEvVR">我对容玦说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2Wl3Mqfa">“快教我下棋！就现在！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3FKXESYh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_WMgiCbq">下了几盘棋，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xjHfsYoL">发现容玦没骗我！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tT709Dy0">我发现自己是个傻子后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XMXp7J5F">心已经凉了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pzxMm2gK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hwNeONEo">最近天天找容玦下棋，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A42cETkK">发现不是下棋凉快，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fwzeuJ-w">是容玦身边凉快。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hnnkNoKT">他，也是个空调成精！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TDTlZqoq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wxBBaF0K">我邪魅一笑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q30BUzcr">哼，太傅只想逃离我！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NHPowzge">男人，你以为我非你不可吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HSlBYxP4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7Dv3CtjP">我使出星星眼技能，对容玦说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hcaZvcI7">“容玦，我最近晚上睡你这好吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qjrpvHUU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nUTNCF8l">容玦：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lnpf7Eew">“好。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oFFQ4QPz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o9KApFyu">我点了点头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_z_EkcB4">并且放下了手中的剑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1yS4prYc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HRqYBJd5">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PDsgNbpV">最近听侍从说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1CaxSpSB">季晏又提刀砍了上次种的树。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gIYfKkYO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2hP9cCdS">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mjdddaCD">我看他就应该发配去大西北种树。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FgTHsaHw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VLCjWte3">消暑，喝自制奶茶。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6E7-tRuz">木杯子铁吸管，茶水加奶放冰块</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tj2d61vu">有内味了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cYH6_c-d">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HYrGtODk">喜滋滋地跑去容玦屋，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Pv7PPQOr">善良的我打算分他一杯奶茶，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8NigGSs3">我绝对不是为了吹冷气。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fT-YpJx1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z-4Y3Kp-">开门，没见到容玦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wGLXUiYY">决定等他。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qnHV6us-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R8t-y7Wf">没一会儿，门外好像有人走近。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6MtffA0n">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6qHiUq2b">我正打算开门，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8e1SNvuf">门却啪的一声被踢飞了</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ocr154Zl">伴着季晏的骂声——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cql3gIcT">“好你个容玦！劝我不要迷惑了，你自己倒是捷足先——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Kkea2baa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z35K2Rts">季晏一踹开门，就看到最近惹他的人站在那里，面带微笑看着自己。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-5KQ_g2M">季晏心下大乱，顿时抿嘴不语。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g07Z_DTG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WdieX4Rf">我身手敏捷地闪过了飞过来的门，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GDBLJpBv">看着季晏，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HoXD8eiu">我忍不住握紧了拳头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MWot1j-A">并露出了核善的微笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lX3B7klw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oFHEpLv0">他、刚刚、踹门</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gNNw56UM">把我放在桌子上的奶茶踹翻了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m6KmjIBr">这他妈我能忍？</p>
 <p data-pid="JgVgiepz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月17</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>众所周知，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6CVgx7xQ">我的报复心强得令人发指。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Mf36MaBL">上一个惹我的人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xtH8kBai">已经被我逼得痛哭流涕。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tYEgeJXa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lOwprK0r">我眼里闪着诡异的光，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1t56WJfr">走到季晏面前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aOIYtw-O">拍了拍他的肩膀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="325ZLBv6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GLCHhpJo">我怀着慈悲心肠问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8sTTqwVS">“你还有什么未完成的心愿吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2hkrfHqC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EBHfUM5u">季晏：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rDOAajuC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N9D-WZCI">看着季晏忍不住后退一步，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sdt8i6rI">却发现肩膀被我牢牢抓住，动弹不得。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MegjNMp4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o1FdjC7Z">我笑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ir0CEE3s">季晏，不要怪我心狠手辣，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="euBwms0N">怪就怪你不应该动它！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vYfUjuKY">这世上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SvQsW2RV">没有人能容忍煮好的奶茶翻了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t2EyKEWD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z8EpR2I1">把季晏五花大绑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6wTL9XSS">扔到他自己的卧房地板上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-cP6-FA1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xTM0vh7E">季晏在地上挣扎着质问我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KFD-1e3S">“钱绥，你干什么！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eFTikRrl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C74F4v-b">瞧瞧，这都急红了脸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RDKEVvRK">可惜，没有人能救你了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YkTXVpNZ">我露出恶魔的微笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="puveeS--">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VOw3CPgz">在季晏惊异的眼光中，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RlghgIlL">我拿起了他平时最宝贝的那把刀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YWZZ0KpW">走到他面前。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Luh-vMuA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fz2Ykavo">看着他惊惧放大的瞳孔，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c14sRHda">真是有趣呢</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3cCIIZoh">———</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DYraHXJO">我：“这是你最喜欢的刀对吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HzCKJtTr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OdvspkAe">季晏：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qxEcUzgj">“你、你要做什么？！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4OIsZiZI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8OwJ3tRT">季晏闭上了眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pwSeogQX">他就知道，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ims1PGW1">钱绥这种人喜怒无常本性难移，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="155BbAVK">可恨自己还愚蠢地以为...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dk6_dPJC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iwNsgA0S">季晏没等到刀落下，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pwB3Mn_7">他睁开眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m-OB1P2U">只看到钱绥在...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8dgXu-pY">反复地摸刀？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MsU8sSrH">？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nLduYQ0h">什么鬼？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1pgshJdG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DIAp875H">“不许闭眼！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q_egr44o">我把刀怼到季晏面前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xtXLgK-5">当着他的面，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9eq5zHBe">开始摸刀鞘和刀柄。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JWX5spSq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mgLwN_XR">看他此刻痛苦万分的样子，我毫无负罪感。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mDgAxwF-">这是你逼我的！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M75z7Tcb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8-PJrVp-">我面色狰狞地说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xBKlEh9E">“季晏，你好好看着！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yU4_za5O">今天，我不仅要摸你的刀还要住你的房子睡你的床！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BZEtWPa3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DRi15hsU">季晏：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6kbSVUio">什么玩意儿？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G5ugmJUV">——</p>
 <p data-pid="8--WPkMb">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ni_82WsR">我着实有些震惊，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AouuqD8K">季晏怎么没有痛哭流涕悲恨万分？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GPwN6-gh">可恶，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n3b8AulO">这竟然还不够吓唬他的吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-kvAJmg3">看样子要加把火了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GFjtDLdD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WgyimJIO">欸？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5TWqTBOE">容玦怎么来这了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0-5vAfa1">既然这样......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LBjkFPoq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Mz8c4qTv">我一把搂过容玦，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TSn81BWW">以迅雷不及掩耳之势</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8Tqw_OAW">啵了一下容玦的脸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HCZm9I8s">然后对季晏说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zZh_bvOU">“不仅如此，我还要泡你的基友！”</p>
 <p data-pid="8zjWWGWT">——</p>
 <h2>7月19</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>我说完这句后，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5QmyRXe-">季晏和容玦愣得像两块木头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_nBb9JlH">他俩不会吓傻了吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9qyGMWsu">不至于吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_Bdn0z5F">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
