 <p data-pid="Nwj-nnRg">反思一下，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d8h7iL4K">我这套堪比打你的孩子睡你的床亲你的老公的报复是有些过分了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bp_W_Lxz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mkLsyDHD">虽然，但是......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LCkIc2zP">我忘不了奶茶的牺牲！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-0vDRJgb">呜呜呜呜</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zMFQKD3F">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m3LZvue0">抓着容玦的肩膀使劲晃，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_It50JVv">我哭得像尔康一样，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7b3oWjqo">“容玦，你知道吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pNAAUT-C">季晏他，把我的奶茶打翻了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CMd3AQhO">那是奶茶吗？是我的命！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xZnRvs3d">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rPgAsECE">季晏：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PDYyBZI1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ajBsYia9">容玦：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KtBtCpID">这个奶茶，约莫就是撒在他房里的不明液体了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MhlBrSaY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0ftxSKs2">沉痛地打击了季晏后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v3hsgl98">我黯然离场。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eoLgI_40">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pOntQTOS">撞到赶来的侍从。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5bCY8I9W">侍从：“大人！容公子回来了！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kjnuOXQN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nTtfZ-P2">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xjbf250u">天翼2G，就是快。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mhDKjlzk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VKvVjYbH">哎，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uLKcRtWP">无论遇到什么，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YEP6CUwO">人都是要活下去的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vbEoymm3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G-kc7PGy">所以我决定...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VZMZDaXU">出去找乐子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hGV8CU7h">抚慰受伤的心灵。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ayS8B4Zh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M-q9qiZf">这次带上侍从。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XDv2ocg4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pmAIH7ER">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f_lg6TLI">“大人......不能再买了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dR3XYf7a">侍从对我说。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R3-FnunK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ngUtgVy7">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mqhU5jB_">我只是买了三套衣服两双鞋两个镯子一盘花三盒蜜饯两袋坚果一盒云片糕两盒桂花糕两盒绿豆糕三个油酥饼两串冰糖葫芦而已。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OTr-9-VR">就这么点，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nFWdn35i">为什么不能再买？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wOFbFMRC">“不会吧？我不会没钱了吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nir39b5U">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C_ZsUhXj">侍从：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tt5i7drh">“不是，是我拿不下了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EiXG9EVA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sNzGcCCD">遗憾地让侍从回府了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xg-mQjdl">我决定再去逛逛。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="02Rt7L7U">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NklvmHO3">嗯？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M8AsQJ96">长乐坊？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JkP4Xrh_">想瞧瞧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XDxgVj6p">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UhBA7K8U">我由着门口的漂亮姑娘拉我进去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y1fKbkgZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DJiWkDwn">嗯？！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7tQ6Qn-N">这什么标题党？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sTHldUdq">长乐坊居然是个赌坊？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aDBK5kHZ">那你放个漂亮姑娘在门口钓鱼呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HMQ5zi13">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DjHqBjA8">漂亮姑娘也不见了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3_kL9dJk">一个满脸横肉的大汉按着指节格叽格叽响，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tfie-T73">粗声对我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZfcKwDcw">“来都来了，不玩一把吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qkyBHw2F">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MNQrwqPD">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z9XlwAp_">“你礼貌吗？在教我做事？”</p>
 <p data-pid="_kTvIS-9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月20</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>大汉明显被我镇住了，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0d8UcXVZ">眼睛瞪得跟门神似的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NPJGkcdE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a_h4fDe_">我本来想暴揍一顿赌坊的人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yXVFYFIG">让他们知道知道</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-CV0qkeW">京城一条街，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xGe6SGty">我才是爹！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PKJ2a526">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TP6cLvWl">但是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5Y_6LF8Z">我竟然该死的被诱惑到了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QNSv2G7j">可恶，好想玩一把。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6fYYoslt">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HzGfMMTH">我一脚踏上赌桌，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="40x3Ivcd">气势凌人地对那个肌肉大汉说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yP1WvmRf">“骰子、马吊、叶子、牌九，你选一个。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d0-Xti7E">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LGc49qb_">大汉：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dFZ6sQeV">谁才是东家？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-xBzj6hu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xvezhr1_">肌肉大汉选了最简单的掷骰子比大小。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZA3JHi1q">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uk3o1fxM">我勾起唇角，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OkWMMvmA">笑了笑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h1anEkxL">小样儿，你爷爷我打四岁起就会摇骰子了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iWaSHBqY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wZ4mgcYL">我自信地拿起骰盅摇起来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7GqCJxEm">叮叮咚咚</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GzKd-XVX">叮叮咚咚</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sC4AATI2">啪一声把骰盅扣在桌面上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Havd_7mM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Lj_EsROo">我：“大”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LrcMnexJ">大汉：“小”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_fqvbtZ_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ck7iERgE">开盅——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WGcvfw6P">小。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cEA8t5YK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Jw5yAplx">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SGbryE80">骰子你像话吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p9VdkUZm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V2pk1RTQ">小失误，不要紧</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="03Y0JyNC">再来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TM1L_Obe">叮叮当当咚咚当当</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qVCLkqJ7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1IirHnTG">我：“小”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6Dob071c">大汉：“大”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9byRB6tT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8zaolaH_">开盅——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9pEhD8cR">大。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ORzXgMAb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bNYZtvNU">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4zcPflc5">小意外，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aw0KU9iX">再来亿回回。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AVsTWG-n">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aX2xBHD1">.....</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eB3UqnML">三十回，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T38alcj0">完败。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rNmGLPOz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AHRqz6PG">不可能，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XsL7wjiL">我不可能这么非！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4nZoLC2g">这特么合理吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1zbn7meL">一定是肌肉大汉出老千！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f0t83Cnf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cKYXpYw7">我揪起肌肉大汉的衣领，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FnhPGnUy">凶神恶煞地怼脸问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OSCnQuk2">“说，是不是出老千？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UosDTTb8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rXdfpi9p">肌肉大汉：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iBTb1BaU">“你自己摇的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QEK1IpL4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8_G-jxY-">我大怒：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K9uoRQao">“你说我倒霉？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SB4ZAJUz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0CZ6z103">大汉：...？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aH49OfPc">“小白脸，你够了啊。愿赌服输，给钱！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nt8YXm0K">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NdpP5_7I">他满脸横肉的脸上露出一个威胁的表情，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N08T6LV0">松了松双拳的指节，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZLJvk1U0">似乎要对我动手了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FGswV0-S">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_jojMaGn">哟，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fTw6T7KZ">要想打架我就不困了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CrSiJj5X">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BIXfHU-5">呵呵，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iNDYUFHt">我对肌肉大汉露出了富有一个标志性核善的微笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f3jLhijj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wWY4VX8K">大汉：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gZkEqkgL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vQ71yOgx">我冲上去揪住他的衣领拎起来就是一顿暴打。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iGa5yH-y">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="05w8QEsQ">“啊、啊啊不要打脸——好汉饶命！......俺靠脸吃饭的！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b-RFePde">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u7oTWdO-">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y5DrRpm8">仔细看了看他满脸横肉带着刀疤像极了青铜神兽的脸，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tNDhZxJh">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9PtvLHR9">没别的意思，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-7-6C9U6">单纯疑惑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A1U1-ODB">得多不挑的人才好这口？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sxipEnKa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JNWhSoQS">大汉鼻青脸肿痛哭流涕地对我说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="frgEJiTI">他欠了赌坊的钱，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ksK6H-ON">只是因为长得凶被赌坊留下来当打手震慑一下欠钱不还的人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="L_XAXNyP">其实平时连只鸡都不敢杀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xz-t5eA1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tl012UAR">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HylWMXkm">“脸上的疤怎么来的？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XfKmj2pU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A-AJgd1b">大汉不好意思地抓了抓头，黝黑的脸上泛着诡异的红。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-NLNK0oI">“走夜路摔倒，脸磕石头上了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5dyT_dRJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OzomH_yj">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f99BDZ2j">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0L4xU-jL">等等，有盲点。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="L2mMYvfV">“你这运气还能欠赌坊的钱？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XkDG1CfI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NGUORp8g">大汉嘿嘿憨笑：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K5FN2l2l">“俺也是第一次遇到你这么倒霉的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uxN8k90U">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p2itvEUG">怒了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I2Dn4Jto">又揍了他一顿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6Y5V7n9f">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HCKy1Gi9">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aN84pt1_">出赌坊，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s-YyxGID">回府。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n-kAV9G3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g3ur-qtD">身后跟了两个人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="he6ob73x">一个漂亮姑娘，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fQNOBRP_">一个肌肉大汉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="owdAnt2X">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uLyqiKP0">提一嘴，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xZz3YM-N">作为京城热心市民，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ji7bLauZ">我顺手向京兆尹举报，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6wrh3KQ5">抄了长乐坊这个黑心赌坊。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I_hHVdgm">我与赌毒不共戴天！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s4Igt-vY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Se4EfNq7">漂亮姑娘和肌肉大汉无家可归，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OhVyKE_y">我就带回府了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lOFD4E_4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x5xRrEIK">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tU7Ii03-">回到府里，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oGz-Yn4_">侍从说，季晏等我好久了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rO51uvoU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wu9KHMg0">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ls3BSRKW">他找我干啥？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DhWq608I">想报仇？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ercFZMtH">他又干不过我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0hdDnlY-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ScYBKjvr">季晏应该是听到我声音了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1e5UmHN8">推门而出。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qY8KntAm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NVZakPv8">季晏一出门就看见了跟在钱绥身后的人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MYRdmuz0">一个容貌秀美的年轻女子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yQ9IqskX">？！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wd0UXqHy">“钱绥！你又去招惹人了？还敢带回来！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vXyK97W0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9q-7Kr5D">突然，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SfOhdzbO">他看到那女子身后还有一个人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nQZgCpRn">季晏忍不住瞪大双眼：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4gV621KP">“原、原来你好这口？！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bRwITGYB">——</p>
 <p data-pid="WrokoZrv">我：？</p>
 <p data-pid="zpVbL6yb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月21</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>不是我说，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QnJjTeN4">季晏脑子里都什么黄色废料？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kE9nMlXB">我像那样的人吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YB7pKgRS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dkpHn1YJ">我伸手捂住了他的嘴，说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sHThAR-L">“不会说话可以不说。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tXNltj_O">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ns2VJEEW">唔唔唔......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pa95Ncfa">季晏挣扎着要扳开我的手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kfamD8UP">而且挣扎力度越来越小。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QLjtX92t">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ir3dqUO5">哎呀呀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KduF_ffc">捂个嘴而已，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NB2bpkhH">至于这么激动吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yGAG5Sin">于是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rAa7uEkt">我又加了点手劲儿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nVsjMw3E">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-FUeEEKB">感觉到季晏安分了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o-54KSg1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="utgy8CB1">肌肉大汉：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rf1IVIwU">俺看不下去了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x5uN7Voa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pORvmzh1">“钱大人，那个...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bSlWNKgx">你好像捂到他鼻子了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K38rLBfP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g-h6e3ft">我：？！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LjQFi4df">仔细一看怀里的人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZRifaR9w">果然两眼快翻白了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g_9U_-Rj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0E-9BUga">我赶紧放下手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DhQD-VVJ">疯狂摇晃他肩膀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gi0Kba5G">“季晏，季晏，你不要死啊！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="02RQEJBP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xgI_eO_V">终于，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k12apVSv">季晏虚弱地睁开眼，唇瓣微动好像说了什么。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JFwZb63j">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="92JBV0Je">人还活着，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BlvwDWyD">我喜极而泣，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h13Vtyca">侧耳去听。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZNbtaxXL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ztS3XvWW">他说：“放...手...不要晃...我要吐了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KGhuiYat">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rERIbS96">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eygzYZsA">哎，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rvtKnMyL">回府时闹了点小乌龙，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C1woAQ3L">不过不打紧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3-vgHeZe">回头再送根人参给季晏当赔礼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YzFeZ9iF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Qx0rJbfB">现在问题是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZlEFHrkS">怎么安排漂亮姑娘和肌肉大汉好呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-yqBYTEO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QMcpbsMC">漂亮姑娘叫......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="69hKbCYk">呃，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_2lLjNhY">我好像不知道哦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lHHSh4BA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EwZO0tXT">“你叫什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KtiWhDS8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qfMy46As">漂亮姑娘白生生的脸上露出几分羞涩，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7i9HM11b">“奴家名唤白莲。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7A5Jl_1k">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vDAL4FVy">啊这？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N4OGD_0b">深深看了她一样，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AfbZzYt8">我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mBbF--Is">“名字不错。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j2Iwt0CV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uwALvA9W">看向一边的肌肉大汉 ，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_prJjjfO">“你呢？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7pYH922Z">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KVaKY0rq">“俺叫小壮！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dUZML7mp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TcYHz4aX">我：这不太小啊。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uLBg0m8O">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wSWx7FRJ">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E2rbxz0f">白莲说她擅长抚琴奏乐磨墨收纳打理等，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RgX-a8vb">我眼睛一亮：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zIELk0jI">“正好我缺个贴身侍女。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zCz0b4yF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XgKxewW6">小壮见状挠了挠头，说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="utveqm9S">“俺......俺擅长吓唬人。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rjAkPVKv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ORsW8zxm">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Bc6ZRVpa">摸摸下巴，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OMTv6ZAN">想到个了好去处。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mhiIXYE5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5GppF1dy">两分钟后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RU4V2Pyk">小壮抱着我的大腿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YuDZQ9Wk">一米九的壮汉哭得像个孩子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yMfKcteC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_wHfMHVk">“大人，不要——哇——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mJZuzugG">俺不要去杀鸡——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p_DsQiOT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_rgbUvCN">我冷酷地抽腿走了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tCAdZfND">呵，不好意思，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y85Su75p">我还记着你说我非呢。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Vu_HJk8e">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HcHHj-hS">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vnPUXQke">不想上班，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4b3Bicnp">天天批奏折，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="11VFN09k">九九六都没这么累的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OKa52HIY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="smcFtWp6">装病请假，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IVS3mnZO">三天没上朝入宫了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IrJnnss2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bmAMtcDh">府里蹲哪哪都好，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Nq65ZOfF">就是有点想捏小皇帝的脸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kUFxHCwc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x7XVmvte">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="beZSet_D">皇宫。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KEJ7EhvR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oBoyKKbb">小皇帝扯了扯太傅的袖子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NhZjIGU3">星星眼技能启动！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UD5qiKin">“老师，我好想义父。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cmLMQU9a">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wUduFNUJ">太傅：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ICdBXNHU">莫名觉得这眼神像钱绥。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BJarDem5">瞥一眼扯自己衣袖的小胖手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t25ABSL2">他冷淡地说：“陛下，慎言。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rK4CFLlq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p_mQ21wo">小皇帝：哼</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_fSiPvId">猫猫委屈，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k_m6ssYh">猫猫生气！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Oj7Z8APw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VDlGhFKd">小皇帝耍赖，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PiKDND4A">“哇——朕不管——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lZPa4YxF">太傅！朕要见钱绥！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-qZcJ8n5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mQnTA2eR">太傅：...？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dfJtWavt">你敢再在地上打滚试试？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U8WQqyAC">是不是跟钱绥学的！</p>
 <p data-pid="85iKz7A1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月22</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>侍从说，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="resiNx_L">太傅到我府上探病了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3anPfaJa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MG-lT-ek">稀客呀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hITsjp9D">太傅竟然会主动来找我？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2koHxzOI">不会是假的吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Pp0Y7IiE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VJIC2OEO">向天发四，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e-HxIl-d">我本来是不想见这个欲擒故纵的男人的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="acTwwgWS">但是我承认他的小花招勾引到我了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M57NDgv5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-gnnBPgf">去客堂瞧瞧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VUNE8KDL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DVBHeOnN">一到客堂，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yhaPqTUu">冷气扑面而来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S-pUIhiL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uxJeTnpF">鉴定完毕，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JIP-uJ08">真·太傅。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XPhNGOxf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kFYrduj1">嗯？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nhxoAI0U">⊙∀⊙！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SeK80Ito">我看见了谁？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="spwWvayC">太傅身后的小豆丁是——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NUc5DQOd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dEK5Yjc8">“陛下——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EgLP6Sq3">“义父——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OliGuR9W">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3IqJMt6J">呜呜呜呜，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y0bd-P87">双向奔赴，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RCmss1Bf">太感动了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ojqGUgNM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QmhAKgZd">我一把举起小皇帝，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9qhwq30o">激动地在他肉乎乎的脸蛋上啵一口。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vYRNrXts">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EMmKVvFi">小皇帝脸红了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cMg9pcMC">好可爱。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0HcZrn8y">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B_Pmz-0P">咦？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aOIdUUtE">太傅脸色不对劲，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ebKz6dwK">看我的眼神里带着三分哀怨七分恼怒。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fP6KE7YW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VW80POIG">这次是真的啦，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iSI99UF-">没瞎编。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XbQLBClF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zOmYMWzX">悄悄问了下小皇帝：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BmXHH83C">“太傅怎么会准你出宫找我？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SwpYnOH9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gTam9oh4">小皇帝搓了搓小胖手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pUjDxqq8">凑近我耳朵小声说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fzlAziG7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NV0W7goP">“我用了义父的招数，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jWNGshQI">黑熊打滚！猫猫挂树！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e2Y7-Ohv">老师就允我来了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l90Um_UV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o9pM7glM">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AfBEFCmn">好像知道太傅的眼神是怎么回事了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MNhBY3Vs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vPMaS0DO">天地良心，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WBXXrWAg">我没教过阿宣，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tZFSuKMF">他偷学的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JnIQNKv8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KO108b3T">哎，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jKAjvgNO">没办法，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WProMOXM">阿宣这孩子打小就聪明。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hflhWTyc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7Zz106dZ">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eyGTlhs-">太傅跟我说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PaPTfTQ1">再不回去，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vzbPo5XY">皇帝就要变成只猴子了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_2vrJPTc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oDbbG_3f">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bUT2xjbU">总感觉他在内涵我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ifd8msJo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B-8wEbOY">无奈上班。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xFw3irz2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MYoDziwQ">！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h9W-A_LH">三天而已，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xPrpigAW">奏折就积了一堆，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mY0Suedi">这合理吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pdx4YShp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a2OHVRtK">翻开一看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zgeV242S">一半是参我本子的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nSESD0S7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gOLigPuE">“宦臣钱绥，好逸恶劳。享朝廷俸禄，不分君忧，实属失职......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QV_mpxM0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lNn3Ovkw">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MOXvVUGL">管事嫌我管太宽，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e12lLc4G">不干又嫌我偷懒？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XDuUFA6H">好想把奏折扔这群人脸上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2Smn2RDX">给爷爬！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SA55YT1n">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PdIFskDn">我看向了一旁</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z1_5XnIo">导致我九九六的罪魁祸首。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MY8Pdwp6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iGeMwE6h">就是你，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p0zfyF8n">小皇帝！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IKrdBbm3">你怎么还不长大！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f82LE1dh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UmtfDbkl">生气地冲过去把他头发薅成鸡窝头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7Ory91ng">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zswEidq6">小皇帝：...？</p>
 <p data-pid="MEnJs3VT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月24</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>事实证明，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mi06s1XQ">欠下的迟早要还的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zKFiM4Er">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FQMZAXhF">我一晚上奋笔疾书，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x8fmlz9P">终于，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="THG1nOqj">把参我本子的官员全都臭骂了一遍。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iUpcVBRo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I67Zgdi6">爽，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cE-LqCyM">这下舒坦多了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZPHG8opo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LHrVMPHQ">小皇帝翻着奏折，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9q6Rt_sT">眨巴眨巴眼，疑惑地问我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="grAzJ1lg">“义父，为什么批红要隔行书写？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9Wuovo25">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oy5NLcqa">“嘘。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D2Z2TPfU">我用食指抵住他的唇，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5e5DRNz2">露出了高深莫测的笑容。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KRUSpbbV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TsTPRcJC">“因为，我任性。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ys5TNtMA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lsZ-799V">没等他若有所悟，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PwrCnsZY">我想起前车之鉴，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="clw9XoFK">又补充了一句，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bMJ-on-L">“你不许学。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B9O6uV8c">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mZiVTk6-">小皇帝：“哦~”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t8OrPL1P">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6A56ck0L">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LJPAQK-U">哎</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h1SglAR-">有些人活着，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AynB9cYv">说是男宠三千，流连青楼，出入赌坊，一掷千金。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6Sk21zW7">其实他已经死了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P9qJseBU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bfCkcbX_">书案上奏折堆积成山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FOOFJPPB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XumhEE8w">我瘫在书案上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pywuSBuw">用腐朽的声带喊出：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y1GdxRp7">“救救我救救我......我需要休假。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dj6_j2bq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SF2r5e_0">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XCsT_cXs">白莲跟在钱绥身边也有一段时间了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TuLEUm4Q">她发现，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qZ-NP-zY">这位钱大人与传闻中不能说是一模一样吧，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5t7L59Ac">只能说是毫不相干。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LQwDiLjk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5hhtOfEp">此刻，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dvTmDK6B">钱大人宛若尸体一般瘫在木椅上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kJTkO_5H">张口说了什么。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cBY_PQXm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XYq8NGmk">白莲放下墨条和砚台，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kgsZ3xOW">附耳去听，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pl8eWc3l">只听到他在说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kUYFfCG0">“白莲......我要不行了......帮我把这些奏折都烧了......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dZWjhAfi">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aOIlC-U7">白莲：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Jon13_dR">这是钱大人本月第二千五百四十一次说自己要不行了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UySMkyfS">至于烧奏折，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j7Ofwdpn">他在说气话，不能信。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B9bGZuGW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4d502FIf">白莲歪头想了想。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6-_e0xxS">突然勾唇浅笑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ebuq5H9a">俯身在钱绥耳边吐气如兰，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MzbPWaWN">“大人，倘若您今日提前完成工作，奴家今晚......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CzcXaGuP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nxaoaV3C">侍从进来书房，看到的就是这一幕。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IR2YAkiT">钱大人伏在案上，微侧着的脸宛若好女，只是眼下青黑，眉间似蹙。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YiFx4v1Y">而美貌侍女白莲的纤纤素手正搭在钱绥的腰间，二人脸凑得极近，几乎贴在一起。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_-jrYvXL">不知白莲在耳边说了什么，钱大人忽就展开了笑颜，端的是色若春晓之花秋时之月。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nGcVs3u6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r7FCqXfp">......真是好一副红袖添香的和谐场景。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LQrMTGBu">侍从这样想。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OW99DpGS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Sac3Z5ln">呃，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6-SYvOfI">如果忽略他带进来的容公子和季公子的话。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_f2R-92o">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uxbnKWOh">容玦：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mSiPPCoy">季晏：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w2B6MIJB">狗男人！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NbtzwDEj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R4NNKXHE">不，钱绥只占前面一个字！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zVHNYN_o">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x_hWSa3C">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Cfzo1JSF">眼观八方，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nLZiuCNz">侍从心下了然。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wNtLgZWo">在白莲和钱绥做出更过火的事之前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7S6U0IfW">他以拳抵唇重重咳了两声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1ynM27-K">“咳、咳、咳！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1Ki3qTDe">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fN277Xzu">大人，属下只能做到这一步了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eTNcR4YH">溜了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ixzv1fuL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oAYAfn8f">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MPZUmaS2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6SOge-NF">门口传来咳嗽声，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VWxMjFNW">我扭头看过去，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="amSw6PWu">只看到闪过的一道残影和两位美人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0kZGxey-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B3fpEtU6">“容玦、季晏？你们怎么来了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V8_ArJeI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eHXbkW1l">嗯？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4gw-3sOA">咋都不理我啊？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PVBB-qhV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O3b0i7Kx">容玦和季晏的面色很古怪，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R0Ve-ztG">具体一点说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6A2xpAch">像便秘了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JBLbYFlP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KQVVjaHl">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r9W5OjK1">白莲的脸色也好古怪哦，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WT6simtz">便秘还带传染的？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3Lcg1Ml-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bhvArthh">你们三个互相瞅啥呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OYefKalf">搁这用眼神舞降龙十八掌呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4vaUO6YK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HAJ-aFRU">达咩！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="foRVLkm9">我伸手捂住了白莲的眼睛。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tilwy3ee">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7i7M8o6W">哇塞，白莲的睫毛好长，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Hmpjw3Nm">戳我手手了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yokN8dI6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KWuz6w26">白莲脸红了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XwKUm70Y">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DiutBBEM">容玦：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wbrAJEkx">季晏：...火冒三丈.jpg</p>
 <p data-pid="ppmbXtS9">你脸红个什么劲？妖女！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CTNVlImY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QzSV-KVx">咦？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NHeGTV5z">我摸了摸胳膊，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pKy5E83P">书房突然有点冷。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1mrvxtf1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gozu4q5O">容玦的制冷技能失调了吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gbc8tdbM">季晏怎么也突然甩袖子走了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XC0q4fwT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B8FRo5k4">？</p>
 <p data-pid="TKFjSaSy">？？</p>
 <p data-pid="uaoATmF8">？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AGvYNa-w">小问号你是否有很多小朋友？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0zWsYlnS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f1BrmUMC">这时，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J0DX3kru">白莲牵起我的手。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="83vTowRc">蹙眉垂目，忧愁地说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XlkiBNXK">“钱大人，你让奴家给你按摩，容公子和季公子不会生气了吧？容公子季公子也真是的，不像奴家，只会心疼钱大人~”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="So6USFO3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QrlcOVbX">我：...？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="onvgrwAy">你是叫白莲不是叫绿茶，我没记错吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ri_O6QZL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月25</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>白莲把头靠在我的肩膀上，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YOvv-HHQ">怯生生地说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f51txZqV">“钱大人，季公子和容公子不会揍我吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wgxQCf5q">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CH7PNe-w">在钱绥看不见的地方，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ImeaG4r1">白莲勾起唇角，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="L_d7XmKG">挑衅地看了一眼容玦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="32jL6cin">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QjRrJeeg">容玦：…呵呵</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BQBslr7h">“容某岂敢。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CU6Wd3K0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-lx2Mwn4">我：？！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vdjw2dzA">救命，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ejO4bJb2">绿茶味儿越来越浓，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wVbPzYuQ">室温也越来越低了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1L2gny0R">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5SLi96hu">为了阻止这场绿茶与冰块的对决，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8pyWPVN_">我急中生智。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6rHtOkYa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LKcirYq0">把仿佛得了颈椎病的白莲扶直站好，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xQOLtqbA">顺手拿起椅背上的外袍给她披上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u25OKQJk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vv2rlVAe">深情款款地凝视着白莲，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w7PKnCjV">我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SfwZVQU2">“穿件衣服吧你。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JRT6Gd33">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cEeZjzs-">白莲：…？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mYwG--8P">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9qZDKUlB">趁白莲发愣，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZmBpY4zj">我扛起容玦就是一个芜湖起飞，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YOLKoeg9">远离了这个是非之地。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eOjGMnc5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FhnesvYK">跑远了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N2yYrWBt">赶紧放下肩上的容玦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oMknXNHH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wpNQoRe8">呼——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2kqXlcpn">人还是新鲜的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t68JwDbx">有点冻手。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rx7WD149">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a5W8WSZD">容玦脸色好像不太好。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I9R-Cziw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C5hioBCD">拍脑袋。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G_aLukMT">哎，怪我</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hz-VmqSD">忘记容玦是个病弱美人了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D56iv89T">刚刚应该扛白莲走的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hvRPbF_j">反正效果都一样。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aktMUdyp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hTU6Wo2T">我挠挠头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mIrVRJWz">怀着歉意拍了拍容玦肩膀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NfuzzYBY">“抱歉，要不我回头再送根人参给你？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cJbIP_Q3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dAw87uBu">容玦拍开了我的手，伸手理了理有些乱的衣襟。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nzITqJ4x">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9yb5ArRz">他皱着眉，俊美的脸上露出我看不懂的神情。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XktY35sz">他看着我，薄唇微动：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n1zYcBa5">“钱绥，你是真疯还是假疯？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AL7ZLYMA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qapDv7R7">啊这，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NI_tOabM">我一时脑子短路了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BY_VAVvI">瞪大了我的狗眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="05y6ZsJw">眼睁睁看着容玦美人转身离去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Nw9wfiwF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zP2U39ER">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XQTWYBSK">完球，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m4IwtHLN">呜呜呜，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="he5ek7xn">好像又惹美人生气了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rgGUZSpj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KkQmVIyS">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KVPAZobC">晚上习惯性地走去容玦屋里。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6qMYd5l9">发现我的铺盖被扔在门口了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tePdgrzu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wWupbzxU">呜呜呜呜，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nuw1stzi">我再也不能享受冷气了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rq1bjzEj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2x3PEPNg">流下了悔恨的泪水。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lKMf9SqY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7dT9ESA1">含泪回自己房间，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PpXMZZ5c">接受了白莲的马杀鸡服务。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1Acd4kYN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GSP1CPXP">别说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JpeWUUYt">白莲这手法，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PpsXznav">还真得劲儿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rwEmuCNG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7Y867YLn">委婉地拒绝了白莲的更多服务，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MP3AZV9x">我抱着竹枕睡了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0k00lIT0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bspUQA1H">没有容玦的第一天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Qx-frDjQ">想他</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZTYfm_F9">的冷气。</p>
 <p data-pid="ln5P-d6d">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月26</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>呃，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="56eOGJGm">美人们闹脾气了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6XkbtLUs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ovbVSpoe">容玦闭门不见人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9hxGxEdG">季晏夸张一些，不仅提刀砍树，还把上次修好的院墙又砸了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qCkolkwg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ABYDY7z0">我没敢去触霉头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YNqhMhoc">只能仰头长叹，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PjdDQsgg">男人心，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FMgnHcNE">海底针。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XXHrGGT9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="naCf4nGh">愁，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bqpRxfe5">想找个人出谋划策。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fHe40w0j">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cr0kwfB6">找谁好呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="al90qTYB">摸摸下巴。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y3y-gMN8">！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P9vNUDxY">有了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-e8UegPy">去厨房找小壮。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a-XR8_-S">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YXuwJi4C">我去厨房的时候，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Go7_idJ9">小壮正被厨房的管事老头追着跑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eX60j7md">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OZN1OEy_">他跑，他追，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7pandG9Z">他们都插翅难飞。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I__bjLd-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NLP5835R">哇塞，小壮跑得好快，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LEjxEcsi">原来体重真的不影响跑步速度。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QyQ_YF0-">厨房管事老头也不赖，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A8akI59J">提着菜刀也跑得很...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gPC_JVTW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CKdBaZ-v">？！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BYar9kT3">等等，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kVRMgrbq">厨房管事怎么还提着菜刀？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HKRcy36h">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-H1SBmbI">小壮看见我了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ki4eWTrw">铜铃般的大眼迸溅出有救了的神采。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2qARUh8j">他冲上来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vB3S3Vu8">猛地抱住了我的大腿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b7_uQl4B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5wCQQvoZ">“呜呜呜——哇——钱大人——你来救俺们了吗——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xUI5Capx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n25yFAJv">我：俺们？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="khi2Q6SI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uJjX4z6-">管事老头也刹住了脚步。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DE66g0BE">见我来，问了声好。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qJo3nowF">然后吹胡子瞪眼，拿菜刀指着小壮就破口大骂：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RqpSlpjN">“钱大人，你知道这混小子都做了什么吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fd1XhQrV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="75Lizbc3">小壮委委屈屈地扯我衣角。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="15eHwion">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RnAOH-9i">管事老头气得眉毛发抖，大吼：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7F6-pI6v">“把你手里的鸡交出来！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c3N6IHH7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zFohKYDC">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IjgG9CfU">低头一看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5kCmJ-jE">小壮一只手抱我大腿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bBM7X4JY">另一只手抱着......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-Zc_a02Z">一只鸡？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5IZ4EaW-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uu6uO_RT">小壮怜爱地摸了一把鸡头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sMTbDLqF">把鸡往怀里藏了藏。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xnd7rSKC">他黝黑的脸上，双眼充满慈爱，粗犷的声音带着一丝柔情。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-yHIOb6e">“鸡鸡那么可爱，怎么可以杀鸡鸡呢？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J3Bw9C82">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5EtBcNGf">我：？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="agzjRcvt">你，可能有点那个大病。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rtqe8svQ">啊，好像我也没资格说别人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O_xbFGwm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZsIILoTA">管事老头气得高血压都要犯了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y6WXh7hH">颤抖地指着小壮控诉道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i12rCS4n">“大人，自从他来了厨房，我们已经一个月没有杀过鸡了！求求您快把他带走吧！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1oBZG5Y_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s-lzlFxf">小壮从我身后探出头来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JQSaRkYd">要跟老头理论，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wMUeK2oV">“鸡鸡是世上最可爱的......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NWMEAe2Y">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mIc1fi0D">没等他说完，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0SD60av9">我伸手轻轻抚摸小壮的天灵盖，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dlglve4z">温柔地说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RqyaRbo-">“闭嘴吧你。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DapF4b4B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-MDIRR6a">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8kqhWmNr">实在没想到，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B3BrO3Iu">让小壮去杀鸡竟成了我的重大决策失误。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LgS2Brog">难怪最近用膳都没有见过鸡肉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DydG_7X5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DmFmwNzO">在老头感恩涕零的目光中，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J75Ka3zq">我带走了小壮，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wWxgFMo1">和他怀里的那只鸡。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1XRfRRyf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nhAClt9V">有点怀疑小壮能不能给我正常的建议，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f99f-dIq">但是来都来了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RSFeSyoN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HgUJO-R7">带小壮去醉花楼喝酒。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8fYBSFwc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TGwrYKBL">小壮皱着粗眉，说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2dcHnaS6">“大人的意思是，白莲与季公子容公子不和？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E3zNAkuN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xSZPK-2A">我点点头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oI1Ofpx7">给自己倒了杯酒。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PBqbyzy7">“而且容玦还问我是真疯还是假疯？你说他是什么意思呢？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H06vGW-J">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qQqx_t6Y">小壮：“要俺说，他一定是在骂你！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OkEqLlSB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xUuHG8Cm">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dGnwVL0h">竟然有几分道理。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lG1-6A-s">但是不能指望这二傻子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qGq2CZJ6">我有二手准备。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zd3TSwaz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PDM1EMat">这不，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PsQqmZgM">醉花楼有现成的咨询人士。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Vz8JIuyh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tTi7nG-z">花魁还是那么好看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ACZAUJoc">漂亮姐姐贴贴。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LxrQ0Os6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gpeWkvV9">花魁美目潋滟，粉面朱唇，素手挽起鬓边青丝，冲钱绥露出个娇柔的笑来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fMKFKePj">“钱大人。”</p>
 <p data-pid="K3Ll2hPU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月27</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>细细算来，自打上回钱绥到醉花楼寻欢作乐到如今，已有月余。</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XzlhfYTO">自从见了钱绥，花魁便害了相思，夜里辗转反侧。更是无人知晓，她的绣枕下藏了钱绥上次匆忙离去落下的折扇。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JzzBqCf6">得知日思夜想的人再次出现，花魁含羞带怯地对镜好生打扮了一番。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="22892XRn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zkKZVL0B">只是她打开厢门，见着那人时发现......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BtUTArKI">他怎么还带了个莽汉来？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RMbZvhOu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="26sbj64O">小壮不知道自己被花魁嫌弃了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Oee7lwOu">还在傻笑着夸花魁好看。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HuedZxWl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V2oeicwy">花魁：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kugdbQgU">算你有眼光。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="btSxnF7x">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dhXxubeN">谁知小壮下一句就是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ADdjQ0t1">“不过俺还是觉得白莲那样的更好看。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cZnRSUAX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kFZhg3fu">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_5EVrLXo">真想缝上小壮那张气死人的嘴，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k_jFvfMv">没事提这干哈？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WoaUi3bX">没看见花魁脸都绿了吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TL3ebwL0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BrnNyM3c">我爆锤了一下小壮，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y9FqZ8wI">拉过花魁说了句好久不见。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s434KGA3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IJbSglBE">花魁面色稍缓，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jN6tsnkA">顺势倚在我怀里，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n70ao2Pe">问道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZQs6gcPH">“大人，不知这白莲是哪位神仙妹妹？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a9CnPfaH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dj2btAt-">“我见义勇为带回府的姑娘。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W-m8W_cr">“钱大人的贴身侍女。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8aaVV_dI">我和小壮同时回答。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UcAHRwph">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gDCVsz7a">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RfkQh-Aq">我特么，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QzhHBEMG">臭小壮，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xxyjTeWQ">信不信我就把你的鸡炖汤喝了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xBX3zv6c">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nsdTCLzk">算了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cD6d87fJ">也不算什么丢人的事。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="woB8WOwU">勉强算得上是后院起火了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aK9fgdL_">虽然我也不知道这火是怎么莫名其妙烧起来的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wnt4cHgL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uONtpxam">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AjaS4kw6">花魁听完我的困惑后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="whT-J65w">欲语又止，默了好一会儿才说道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pcLW1Avi">“恕奴家直言，这容季二人......不过是恃宠而骄，岂有妻妾给夫君脸色看的道理？倘若是奴家......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wqQMxYWT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jFK34vd8">我：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ARA9_hkb">等等，夫君、妻妾？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="83mCGU5_">花魁的话点醒了我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1P9yHaLD">我好像懂了，解决问题要找到根本矛盾，教员诚不欺我也。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OntF6mAw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CGGPwO5Q">男宠什么的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZuWuXkXN">容季二人肯定也不喜欢当吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TnHq6V_Q">趁早各回各家各找各妈不就啥事没有了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xIHH3SfE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EP7g1f7g">“你说的对！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PzM32QjH">我恍然大悟，说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M8mLim4k">“其实......我与他们算不得什么夫君妻妾的。他们......迟早是要得自由的。况且......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jmH-WZJw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VOYYJYST">我看了看自己的某个部位，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="diWkk6Mi">“况且我这样的......的确也不能耽误人家！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VEz-tFzK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SCOYjKgB">花魁：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vraxzqZU">你懂什么了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uMpXiJyo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MsdgR9Ee">看花魁一脸懵的样子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VqEoCaI-">我挠了挠头，不好意思地说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lJeO20Iz">“花魁姐姐还不知道吧？我其实，不是男的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RHeADi2t">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SIYAZh94">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BCoNW1g9">花魁杏眼圆睁，有些不敢相信。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wc_pJh8F">他......竟不是男子？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C2Ie5qCj">自己念了许久的良人竟不是......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YMqzooxH">花魁抿着丹唇，眼波流转，心思百转千回。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nP7jfGFf">最终，咬咬牙。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zgPzhmH9">罢了，女子......也不是不行！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zmRzXopy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UE1yyb7D">花魁笑了笑，伸出葱白的手指，在钱绥的胸膛上打圈儿，说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bne0ZWXx">“什么男子女子，奴家也不甚在意这些个。不过要说后院里，男子终是不如女子温柔可人......钱大人说是不是？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ljJMpBfw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KpTAoAM0">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sPd1VxBB">怎么扯到这来了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QidN_U1w">她一定是误会了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9HEkKsKE">我抓住花魁给我挠痒痒的手，说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o5E1C_0_">“内个，我也不是女子。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="30IHtppq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9o4PD7_T">花魁的手一僵：？！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I-045jd4">也不是女子？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9ox6tLv4">难道是......太监？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iE81O5Vk">花魁再咬咬牙，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hsufD6Ux">她在醉花楼学的花样多......太监也不是不行！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="50l9hYle">——</p>
 <p data-pid="TfDHHcDH">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7Yp4O0Pa">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u_g8HjMW">花魁姐姐的脸色好奇怪，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cRHizlV5">变来变去的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="05H1SqGh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m2DVnU2m">小壮好像也这么觉得，凑我耳边说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U1kAgjZO">“钱大人，这花魁是不是病了，脸上五颜六色的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TALp_s1W">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dVufSe-m">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dxvCymwz">总之，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="znHP6Inp">醉花楼服务很到位，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dFkDnmcj">成功解决了我的问题。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rH4TZL3t">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S6fhjSzr">答应了花魁姐姐下次再来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hpx9Q-OX">我拖着醉醺醺的小壮走了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JCzG9xNU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LKrBUM2e">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EDyhunvr">第二天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9KNU3Tda">我翻墙进容玦院子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="umOlCrcZ">站在他房门前。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IVdHHdxw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KK0trF5Q">妈耶，有点紧张。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0ICl6yE6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oqt5geAB">深呼吸，准备喊：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uGauoj7_">“容......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jMmmf9u-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JSv-EZr8">不行，还是好紧张。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eMxuH_4Q">万一他不开门呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I9iNGAid">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dR8z3oCb">不管啦，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5SZGKYkk">豁出去了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j-yuveik">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8aNbLMI4">我猛拍几下门板，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AVjj0561">气沉丹田，喊道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yAjyT2gt">“容玦，你别躲在里面不出声，我知道你在家，你有本事关门，怎么没本事开门哪？开门呐，你有本事关门，你有本事开门呐。开门开门快开门，别躲里面不出声，我知道你在家！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CeXnwctj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wy9kPzhS">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kTi3Yn4T">正当我准备继续喊时，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OUIcrF2J">门吱呀一声开了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QtvboF0O">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VlGwz_kR">季晏一身红衣，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MjpTwLpC">咬牙切齿地对我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YaVYdizC">“钱、绥！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NuhEVERQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KI1rGdpQ">！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7UGXhHCr">啊这？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5C_S2Qvz">我敲错门了？！</p>
 <p data-pid="1qIWq9jn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月28</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>我对季晏露出一个礼貌的笑容，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pyQ2X21q">“哈哈哈，好巧啊，你也在这？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x72mxFnz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xwRSEGRg">季晏：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0T7xGMj4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0kI7Bneu">糟糕，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZE5QMiuB">季晏把门框捏碎了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rWQlTald">我现在说走错了还来得及吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b8NVCv_b">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yalCd9Nj">后退一步，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bwgAyZ2q">我看到了旁边被砸坏的院墙。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uh6XHu_g">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A15AkaxD">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4HfoX64y">好像真的走错了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D5VWxWw_">这也不能全怪我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QvNABfGg">第一次翻墙，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AAEGnqTn">路还不是很熟。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PYX22eEX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o5sOJgkf">见我后退，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UQi2RU7w">季晏冲我伸出了魔爪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WVgOYnhR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ua5DV5EI">危！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P8eZZbB_">我不想和他打！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sGC4priH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WRdc0r1z">金蝉脱壳技能启动！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ccS0aiyF">我乱指了一个方向：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uqwbKb_m">“季晏，你看，容玦！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-GLsicgp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HhetkvbF">趁他扭头去看，我麻溜地跑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v-npMLSM">“拜拜嘞你！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w8EZ2Lpz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eb2buHCh">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jGzM9WtX">属实没有想到，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4rzqp3D8">季晏虽打不过我，轻功还挺不错的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hBP05g4J">他已经追着我绕府邸跑了十圈了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DQY_WHbf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="089t_NNp">好累，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OVU7wMha">呼——呼——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EDaGXDZh">我停下喘了口气，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k3TyMdd1">看向身后的红色身影。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0oWM_nrb">“十圈了，你...不累吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5ngfzUv_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4XPXJPwy">季晏也气喘吁吁的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zt3YIHvn">扶着墙说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C8o5oBmy">“我...一点...都不累。钱绥，你又跑什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PYLDxFpg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iuaY-JAM">我：？</p>
