 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aB7QByQE">“不是你要打我吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M43z2_6K">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e29jo4Y_">季晏：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="82oVc8ZP">“我打你干嘛？你有病啊？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-5PzRWqe">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZS9gENOV">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xuRrnnyO">是哦，果然我有病。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NpZRDMX-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hKV20Ln_">既然这样，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b1B2el2d">太累了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CNpzN48r">先靠在墙边歇会儿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MpfSFrIk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VaxZdSi_">我喘息未定之间，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S43OC-Xg">一个手掌扣住了我的手腕，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x8rB_2xY">季晏不知何时到了身侧，对我露出个阴恻恻的笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Grv6Ozww">“抓到你了，钱绥。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pdLi5QbX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0eFeMIep">我：！？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zzCLaS1a">这也太狗了吧！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1QFDdrKe">他钓鱼！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="13z8F3sY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="55Do3jr_">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n8JGPKJg">季晏拽我回了房间，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ffyTDG-I">用好几根麻绳把我俩的手捆在一起。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6RiRW-10">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WPZyl8mo">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YcJDjyIY">家人们，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BbxJvRoy">这种场面我也是第一次见。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E43wKqMN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nuA9B2u2">我咽了咽口水，说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o_rLzU0e">“没有必要没有必要，我不跑了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mOSvLW-b">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3dfoprL_">季晏根本不听我的，捆得正起劲，比划着绳子，似乎还打算把我脚踝也绑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="imao02Zy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ooTlfjMe">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ctvx8C3s">认命。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hm5xVjVz">“你打吧。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q925L7Sc">话说我除了灌他喝酒罚他种树修墙当他面摸他的最喜欢的剑亲他基友睡他床和差点捂死他......也没有做其他惹他生气事吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bu4s7hfh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uRCTnWQd">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LpLYGL46">好吧，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v8okVkCD">我都想打自己了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="58eL-wLb">我捂住了脸，发出哀嚎。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9vTwOs_n">“不要打我的帅脸就行了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RNXFaKYQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LpU1_Nz0">等了好一会儿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KSlN6OWr">没动静。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JUDpZpEn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EIbva4rv">从指缝里偷看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LT-Ghq76">正巧对上了季晏在看我的眼睛。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C9eR_CL0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0wdrctOn">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rQX6d9zs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="avcOZ4Er">季晏轻笑了一声，拨开了我捂脸的手。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Jz1rWiA5">此刻，他往日里总是带着锐气的凤眼带着难以揣测的意味。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Njytawm5">他笑着说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M_nB_hwq">“打你？我为什么要打你？”他撩起我的一缕头发，缠在手指上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gH3gj4L4">“钱绥，你总是跑。那次去醉花楼也是，这次也是......不过，这次你跑不了了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g9XXgnzE">他又伸手摸了摸绑着我和他的手的麻绳，然后歪头对我笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="44arotEb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kDLXUOG-">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FoDHXeuN">我有罪，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uwv9Z0On">季晏属实是被逼变态了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xB3A0D-_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VJxOD5bd">秉承着子不教，父之过的理念。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b2tZQ_Ec">我反手就是把季晏绑在椅子上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e6FqcqoI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zgRHDsel">对上他瞪圆了的凤眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NwIf7gfa">我笑了笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ryZihf_D">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="49bq-28h">不会吧不会吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ech61qnX">他不会真的以为我不还手是不行了吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rg6Dq7G0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zSfxfdPm">我给过你机会打回来了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BbWPrXxz">你自己不珍惜的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zXfFPxFp">不要怪我......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BczubuhZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wvpMc_V2">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nhyKvy77">趁小壮不在，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0IYApSgZ">我偷偷拔了他养的鸡的一根尾毛，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OPBTOrX5">再跑回季晏房间。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UMges9r0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jRQX9xuA">推开门。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fVdk8104">季晏被我绑在椅子上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HncJk1Hl">衣衫凌乱，面色狼狈。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g0jcyaYg">“你、不要过来！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="F5GmXhGd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="47pfeShW">我如恶鬼般桀桀地笑着。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z3wXBE0v">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uCfxHkBV">“哈哈......哈哈哈......快住手......钱绥哈哈哈”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1AmOWlPY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W3dEVFEl">“让你绑我，让你绑我——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-DJd8l_r">我脱了季晏的鞋袜，用鸡毛挠他脚心。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pFx5k_xI">哼，男人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LQFpOOvO">这就是惹怒我的下场，面对我雷霆般的盛怒吧！</p>
 <p data-pid="ohRDYvYe">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月30</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>俗话说，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gyDwVB3n">人在做，天在看。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p4L3uFqn">我在做，容玦在看。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aSrpTMwJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AYZxKA_m">“你听我说，我真没有什么奇怪的癖好。挠他jio心，是因为他刚才绑我......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8uPBDo44">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e-TM372r">我把拿着鸡毛的手藏到背后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WEPoiF48">心虚地看了一眼站在门口的白衣美人 。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UJidKSO4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rDTFsxtB">容玦：...面无表情.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AFxNghag">你看我信你吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yYfBKQky">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gLBliihu">看容玦的冰块脸，我就知道他不信。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H2OBE4z4">奇了怪了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IuxVMXTp">我也没迫害过几次季晏，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mibxuXJW">咋总让容玦撞见呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e_DViO35">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="52y64Ftw">难道说.....</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OdLYUgim">他在季晏身上装了GPS？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2skeZgDE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ierv5AKa">为证清白，我戳了一下季晏，说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bnZ2Ttwf">“季晏，你说是吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RPdbEjmR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z8GWuX0Z">季晏从容玦推门进来开始就像掉线了一样，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_O351dDz">被我一戳倒是回神了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VMyfw7X2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1-qPpIs0">季晏面色绯红，眼神漂浮，看一眼我，又看一眼容玦，语无伦次地说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bLtEj-vY">“那个、容玦，你不要误会，我们、我们什么都没做！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FewfTvjV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lcH5yzDH">我：...？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9XhC2fa-">你在说什么猪话？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6set6VYl">解释了，又好像没有解释。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HCAWkXMM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bdjXd2s-">容玦脸黑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7HCeD1mh">容玦转身走了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZyCH_u8Z">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ENMKL9z2">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VYQ6E2G1">没来得及解散后院，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hcgwt4s6">我被抓去加班了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uOKrxAnQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KN74gm_W">皇宫。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="arl3ddeM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V9gKEjbY">我抓着奏折，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="heCYPLXo">差点薅秃了自己的头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p4qD3eqP">蜀地地动？豫州水灾？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="L9qfQfUe">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n2XApKEF">召集官员开紧急会议。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0K3w5jXa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BcpU_moM">“......臣以为疏浚河道，运粮救灾，迫在眉睫......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BIaVlRLx">“......蜀地多地龙翻身，蜀民多受其扰，臣以为保灾区蜀民果腹之余，应派遣能人异士做法伏地龙......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1eiWg6gV">“一派胡言！地龙一说未得证实，何苦派人愚弄百姓......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BcH5ctdc">“陈尚书！你——......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CLlN5jkp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4EnCizO_">这群人你一嘴我一嘴的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7iMVStzV">听得我脑壳痛。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FvI08uqs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dl4vms3b">我看了一眼坐在上头的小皇帝，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T6cGC6p7">他瞪着圆溜溜的眼睛，不知听进去多少。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PhUXLO81">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kJ0JJkgT">散会了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aSCkhT0g">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="26qPrjQl">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HexF8suI">本来要回府的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ImsUSpkH">但是架不住小皇帝水汪汪的大眼睛可怜巴巴地看我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZRYyVEJU">“义父，我害怕......地龙......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bItL5_wT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vUmXULRO">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fOMzRLhh">蜀地离京城远着呢。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J9gthblv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bm8jD62G">没办法，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2npYfeuc">宠着呗，还能咋滴。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1A-oKU8k">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="efqT3RZv">哄小皇帝睡觉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FMZkhV-T">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VwhWJtuH">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l0AUH9WQ">“然后呢然后呢？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wA_CQTE4">“......呃，然后变形金刚和神奇女侠联手，使出七十二变和九阳神功打趴了地龙，地龙被镇压在雷峰塔下不得祸害人间，从此蜀地人民过上了幸福的生活......”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PENPTSSl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_Nz8ftX4">小皇帝面上挂着心满意足的笑容睡了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D0Mg2GaD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s0PpU8z5">我喝了口茶润润嗓子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OjAh2ekv">小孩子好难哄哦，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NQBOa2Oa">要不是我有两把刷子真应付不过来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="finB2X-B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>7月31</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>秃，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fQfjd1w0">头秃，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0_8JN71e">很头秃。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EHiU5qQo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8_CHCsEH">连续加班好几天了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LMP-W5di">彻夜听一群老头辩论，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wYQX5dSO">最后还得整合各种方案。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tITXEBCx">我喜提一副熊猫眼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QtIsAeBI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KJSGj6Bg">不过加班还是有福利的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YQa0-uyW">比如，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9aFfyRfa">可以看到帅太傅。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SCboOZ67">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qXp_zlhm">太傅站一群糟老头之中，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MLAmN2ZT">帅得闪闪发光。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KCt39OAC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M2DzCRhf">爱了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vJEr9I3m">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ieYuQnw4">我露出痴汉笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3AmZ1zgW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R-UB3MUb">“钱大人？钱大人？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ywAnNqjd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C-pfcr-b">有官员小声喊我，我回神过来抹了下口水。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vvj-5Usb">“嗯，干嘛？散会了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4ZW2w7lz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RaGaBLXZ">那官员却不语了，疯狂对我挤眉弄眼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GnwwHl_k">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0u6FJR0i">我：咋？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="szXmKT7Q">眼睛抽筋了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VUg-mevD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o44J0uwr">厅内一时间有些安静。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q3GLvYZj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8zS4VYRi">太傅俊眉修目，高贵冷艳地看着我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5vWFe25K">“钱大人以为钦天监监正所言如何？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7IcGatHF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hmG-bCzf">我：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-6JMWwZh">救命，钦天监监正说了啥？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k_TPEsrx">为什么太傅说话这么像老师点名提问？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D1TLqA1W">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v3LVgscO">“......我觉得他说得还是有一点道理的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mANNHJr0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SuVcGc0w">众官员哗然，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OIucgiCi">太傅冷笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hkusJxEQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o5w6TTGB">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="poYQXCLP">？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pHROLMTk">？？？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b9GCmG_4">好像哪里不对劲，发生甚么了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lXYQi1Li">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qz5NiHlN">看一眼钦天监监正胡岩，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XvWPe_tS">胡岩鬼鬼祟祟偏头不敢看我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DcO-M2Id">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MbDHxDv9">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2jU3OGXe">散会。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yWq-ig4b">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BJ5YusQ5">胡岩跑得比谁都快，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tJo9mr4v">只能揪一个幸运儿问问了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V8NY8WeU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MLHK4-Ws">幸运官员：...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y6jS5GPI">这幸运给你要不要啊？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VirpGJhb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="656uC1Yp">我：“胡岩说了什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="max8u-br">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gpD-imwj">官员眼神躲闪，磨磨蹭蹭地说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_LCmZ2SG">“胡大人说......今紫薇星暗，荧惑光芒大盛，凶兆也......逆臣当道惑君心，天怨降灾，清君侧则山河安泰......灾星不除，社稷难安......扶乩请神，曰，灾生金银中，祸从安定出。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AH_dB4wW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z4Rr7rcm">金银是钱，安定是绥。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BqRpf_ba">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bmhMuVU6">淦！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cX1h6m16">狗胡岩，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8Xy3Gh_S">瞎逼逼一堆，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ff_a10o8">合着在这说天灾怨我？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KMntufuF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6N5NFA0U">老子辛辛苦苦加班加点，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BdseV5we">竟然有人黑？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pt_GQfvy">好气！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aFejQnBD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KF7MRpbf">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="m2WCrJHY">夜里气得睡不着。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GjxsXZ9p">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="28HRt97t">从床上诈尸起来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2wg0CWNn">整一身黑衣，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4PtZGMkI">偷溜进胡岩府邸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9iF2MbSa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qNN_hc5v">趁他熟睡，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Asjt8sPR">捂嘴胖揍了一顿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TzBVnBad">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jgGJG00o">爽了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-xESIlLw">回府睡觉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_qQ3Enqy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uSZdZmsv">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mhegLjxA">早朝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2qsh2LuE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i1M4NZ1S">胡岩鼻青眼脸肿的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8cD1WMk9">配上他的大肚腩，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gJF8oh4A">像猪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E4P4HJLz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9RM2i3kj">噗，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ziE2f82m">差点没忍住笑出声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eVNmhCIa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sZmcbRL-">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ruLkDu3-">下朝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aeHSXuXo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ge9l7XBU">我从胡岩面前走过去，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HRsvEE3g">高傲地哼一声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2z0JdCm4">哼╯^╰</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="L5tyrGp3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9syccljK">胡岩飞快地跑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KzfJT-QS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QBoMtOwT">...</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WATq0SC0">我被太傅拦住了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8u9CUKAf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MsrZES3_">太傅扯我到角落，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dvSJ9Lbi">似笑非笑问我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H4KEDkLN">“钦天监胡大人之事，是你所为？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="79Q81L8-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1-T2Nq4W">呵，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GV00Eysp">这人昨天还提问我来着，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="opPeYIuM">以为我是阿宣吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YEcRqY_K">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d9idNBjD">我冷艳地别过脸，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ViVXSPip">说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pv2GEY2C">“靓仔的事你少管！”</p>
 <p data-pid="aQAuJwu-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>8月1</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>太傅可能不知靓仔为何物，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="inQeegv9">疑惑地看我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NHAMZaJ7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pj-Mjh9E">我冷哼一声，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="evBM76w3">“像我这样风流倜傥玉树临风英俊潇洒风度翩翩的人，你少管！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6TVJ5OSJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rmpbp3Nx">太傅抿嘴。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WDLDW1kQ">太傅笑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ihPppH7Z">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E3ga8K1I">我：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CXrwsjWN">你不要以为自己有两分姿色就可以嘲笑我了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MMEKtGIm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GKzq0WtJ">生气气。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9XvQO6Ny">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tj30W9M3">气消了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CiIwDbiy">没法子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dXzHJAIj">他太好看了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7sAD5Hwy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jgNt_na8">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g0G_5pRK">和太傅去钦天监堵人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RIw_XwHT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VNCdkQtm">被拦了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-WT722Jp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CJBut75I">友善地把拦人的侍卫请到地板上休息。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X_fB7gLo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AodVU3MC">找到人了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YY69EO-j">肥头大耳的胡岩后退到墙角，瑟瑟发抖。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i0LA6tEb">“钱、钱绥，你不要乱来！这里是钦天监！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="poHIyNQl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lZzWQuef">我故作震惊道：“钱某怎么敢乱来呢？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j1RmbjpZ">戳了一下他的大脑袋瓜子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wKrjUoFo">我笑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wCjHaOT8">“胡大人这脸上的伤也是别致得很，谁下手这么风趣？是您家老爷子吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n_otUWcz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BMqKnH6G">胡岩可能第一次见识阴阳话术，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BdGl6YWQ">接不上话啦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n1Juzxsg">只一个劲儿摇头，结结巴巴说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="biLmcAw4">“钱绥，你放过我吧！我只是......推算出来的，没乱说！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VhSk7YvY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7jCm4uuP">爷笑了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fQjB5l8g">你那算卦占卜，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8M9qtLp5">连天气都算不准，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mWVdHynq">还好意思说我是灾星？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0N_BP3U6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mlmEnWmq">撸袖子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Krv7OunB">准备教他做人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8mWh7oFV">我要让这孙子知道什么才是真理！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w0UBO4-W">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NQXOoaTl">正要动手时，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Hre5s-dG">太傅从门外走了进来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4x2VR8DO">清冷的眉眼间好像有些无奈，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FolGIZAd">“钱绥，要有分寸。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Lz-2bHsC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dEniESm1">我比了个OK，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="abyyQHde">“保证能治好没后遗症。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s8M6Ea77">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QZ7VCX3y">胡岩见到太傅，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gM9oeuO0">痛哭流涕地求助：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wkNw-SSy">“太傅救我——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6dgNvQwh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rzjWqcJx">当胡岩的面把太傅推出门外，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kz9-DRS6">关上门，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oBodaoMV">我对胡岩露出八颗牙齿的标准微笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a3wnPdHr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gd3SHkOd">瞧瞧，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2u9yaGWL">这绝望的小表情多有趣啊</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nylLBrCc">我笑着说对胡岩说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="P86KxAUz">“你叫破喉咙也没人会救你的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vCOyrTTu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cnxS8cSu">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8xB8WDG1">我推开门时，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M4e6_D7G">只见到太傅背着手在廊间远眺，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IvPV8KJv">清俊的背影如遗世独立的仙人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3EDIo3fu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A-knFF2y">他听见开门声，回头问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="od_8WTXs">“结束了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DBhHFDsd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cFcK78WT">我点点头：“嗯。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t4_AquXx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wBXS4V-J">“那走吧。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-mz6hIRG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kypjbBPo">我被胡岩跟上拦住了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jEvBTe0V">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MrOIJBGm">太傅见到胡岩没缺胳膊少腿好像有点惊讶。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xkj1A7cj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8A1Tk5FQ">胡岩看了一眼太傅，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EeL3fjdV">然后苦着脸地问我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5pNmA8wV">“钱大人，您忘记说抄几遍了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lF32dtqa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C-hse3Mh">我摸摸下巴，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CIa86gk3">说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i-wJ-72E">“我说过的每句抄三十遍吧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fKMKZMkL">还有，明天我抽背物质的含义、意识的本质、物质与意识的辩证关系还有联系的性质特点。如果到时候背不出的话，呵呵。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bU8EHZpl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Hpha6LJw">我松了松拳头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ueIG2AkN">笑着继续说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p1_4ketf">“如果我发现你抄少抄漏或者找人代抄......呵呵呵呵呵呵”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FvtmbITX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LiTEpQgs">胡岩眉毛一耷拉，差点当场跪了：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-h0ULcFP">！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x4C2nPJV">“臣不敢！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cfS2bXDo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MDmNEWFt">太傅：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cJCaMkVc">他们在说什么？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>8月2</h2>
 <h3>“背得不错。”</h3>
 <p data-pid="i7OTuQX5">我拿着戒尺轻拍几下掌心，</p>
 <p data-pid="lx5zrUBf">问胡岩：</p>
 <p data-pid="SvVY4L09">“知道你哪里错了吗？”</p>
 <p data-pid="P0Br12xK">——</p>
 <p data-pid="T7Sy_ale">胡岩：！</p>
 <p data-pid="cI9cO3Ul">“封建迷信不可信，占星算卦不科学！”</p>
 <p data-pid="E3SzzHk8">——</p>
 <p data-pid="2Fm6GBrN">我满意地点点头，</p>
 <p data-pid="NYlvQve0">孺子可教。</p>
 <p data-pid="A2XJ1OXn">——</p>
 <p data-pid="DpleYFYF">……</p>
 <p data-pid="3MxkjuvZ">满朝上下忙了一段时间，</p>
 <p data-pid="xzZpdS-o">蜀地和豫州之事告一段落。</p>
 <p data-pid="KXJisWOF">——</p>
 <p data-pid="i80TSTUI">得闲了，</p>
 <p data-pid="OLebbb3r">想玩。</p>
 <p data-pid="esohIoyd">——</p>
 <p data-pid="vIQzXVvz">邀太傅去逛醉花楼，</p>
 <p data-pid="tTXP_-Uf">顺便看看花魁姐姐。</p>
 <p data-pid="AJAefRd7">——</p>
 <p data-pid="x0LF9eix">被拒绝。</p>
 <p data-pid="SRcFx9fw">——</p>
 <p data-pid="bK_3_ngN">嘤嘤嘤嘤</p>
 <p data-pid="r6iclBpw">——</p>
 <p data-pid="C56ebAKh">不去就不去。</p>
 <p data-pid="qzAdJ80X">我自己去。</p>
 <p data-pid="H1823fV3">——</p>
 <p data-pid="nIiWmu5y">到醉花楼门前，</p>
 <p data-pid="PAlrY1OO">想起重要的事。</p>
 <p data-pid="lAggGm27">忘解散后院了。</p>
 <p data-pid="RW50kHkS">——</p>
 <p data-pid="_VU1xIwV">来都来了，</p>
 <p data-pid="W3aWTvRf">先玩玩。</p>
 <p data-pid="nvshciXa">——</p>
 <p data-pid="s5CX6Tyv">花魁姐姐越穿越少了，</p>
 <p data-pid="x0dSPpmf">怕她感冒。</p>
 <p data-pid="S1uYBC9-">脱外袍，</p>
 <p data-pid="T9_WJQT0">给她裹上。</p>
 <p data-pid="5fUJL4Ls">——</p>
 <p data-pid="SpYsXdyv">我真贴心。</p>
 <p data-pid="WOk90mO6">——</p>
 <p data-pid="GSylRLsW">听曲儿听烦了，</p>
 <p data-pid="NniMpvTe">教花魁斗地主。</p>
 <p data-pid="UwE8n74T">三缺一。</p>
 <p data-pid="AzbEYmmj">——</p>
 <p data-pid="_FnUrQlF">要不去找老鸨来？</p>
 <p data-pid="6FBHaJbo">——</p>
 <p data-pid="7mLSP6XW">门被踢开了。</p>
 <p data-pid="609AN_3n">——</p>
 <p data-pid="5Vs1KV4F">太傅，怎么又是你？</p>
 <p data-pid="JUsA0vh7">我告诉你，</p>
 <p data-pid="DQMzpwkZ">这次门的维修费算你的！</p>
 <p data-pid="_9cgrn6r">——</p>
 <p data-pid="sdHP1QGI">拉太傅斗地主。</p>
 <p data-pid="BmIy2sRC">——</p>
 <p data-pid="_ZqdDxg-">哈哈哈哈哈哈哈哈哈哈哈</p>
 <p data-pid="gBphftv5">太傅一局没赢过，</p>
 <p data-pid="vCX7ssGJ">这也太逊了。</p>
 <p data-pid="6MK1sfVQ">——</p>
 <p data-pid="CW6NgG4c">花魁姐姐笑趴了，</p>
 <p data-pid="9dJ90PIL">倒我怀里。</p>
 <p data-pid="hWGZUD7y">——</p>
 <p data-pid="wRcLMJPm">太傅脸黑了，</p>
 <p data-pid="6Ubi-Tf_">拉我过去。</p>
 <p data-pid="3zGHFVH7">“再来！”</p>
 <p data-pid="agnYq7ty">——</p>
 <p data-pid="MRA-R0Ob">又十局了，</p>
 <p data-pid="7LraJyXC">他还是没赢过。</p>
 <p data-pid="bdNwFCrS">——</p>
 <p data-pid="rBOhNMUl">原来这就叫，</p>
 <p data-pid="7ucOkYCh">又菜又爱玩，</p>
 <p data-pid="UfGMvLFa">哈哈哈哈哈</p>
 <p data-pid="Z1nNg0Gc">——</p>
 <p data-pid="aXe3cIw4">怕太傅把自己气到冻晕，</p>
 <p data-pid="gJWa8sfE">也不忍心让醉花楼变成冰花楼。</p>
 <p data-pid="U4VvdrXf">——</p>
 <p data-pid="QS-6TJUc">带太傅走了。</p>
 <p data-pid="uf8bCbXd">——</p>
 <p data-pid="TbowIFwX">和花魁姐姐挥泪告别。</p>
 <p data-pid="fuNdnVXG">——</p>
 <p data-pid="w0FvGlX3">太傅全程释放冷气。</p>
 <p data-pid="SB7ffwHX">——</p>
 <p data-pid="s42XDQ8Q">回府。</p>
 <p data-pid="R-qu3T_K">……</p>
 <p data-pid="GOTxJtCe">——</p>
 <p data-pid="EFn2hq7L">我先到家，</p>
 <p data-pid="N-YRXfHG">下马车前，</p>
 <p data-pid="tKptb4g8">象征性地问问太傅：</p>
 <p data-pid="dwWTtdnI">“要不要去我家喝杯茶？”</p>
 <p data-pid="qUvZmSn0">——</p>
 <p data-pid="Ay9Rk0t4">太傅：“好。”</p>
 <p data-pid="eIGfh2Sl">——</p>
 <p data-pid="VXF4f08_">我：？</p>
 <p data-pid="k6ig_l-q">啊这，</p>
 <p data-pid="gpY2GBU5">你认真的？</p>
 <p data-pid="obikwPPS">——</p>
 <p data-pid="l4Yue-7r">好吧。</p>
 <p data-pid="3DfwDwK0">——</p>
 <p data-pid="YBGpT1AT">带太傅参观钱府。</p>
 <p data-pid="zC__8eub">——</p>
 <p data-pid="iolT2ZJl">碰上在耍刀的季晏。</p>
 <p data-pid="KNqhizQI">——</p>
 <p data-pid="fLLhfL0f">季晏看见我们，</p>
 <p data-pid="cIxDOHul">停下了动作，</p>
 <p data-pid="WzIpKGKP">凤眼微眯，嘴角一勾，</p>
 <p data-pid="egHR5rm4">“怪不得许久未踏入后院，原来是有了新欢……”</p>
 <p data-pid="sTMx_HZ9">——</p>
 <p data-pid="px02aHC5">我：！</p>
 <p data-pid="t1Yj5yrE">一个瞬移冲上去捂住季晏的嘴，</p>
 <p data-pid="AOUlkwgb">小兔崽子真会给我找事。</p>
 <p data-pid="5DFxl6YI">——</p>
 <p data-pid="izk8hzWc">我回头对太傅笑了笑，</p>
 <p data-pid="-PQ1m9ES">“哈哈哈，犬子无状，胡言乱语。见笑了。”</p>
 <p data-pid="cSp1onxV">——</p>
 <p data-pid="7zteRCLi">太傅冷眼一瞥，</p>
 <p data-pid="yXaNxnDK">对我说：</p>
 <p data-pid="lxmsph4f">“令郎……岁数比你都大啊。”</p>
 <p data-pid="09wV2yRY">——</p>
 <p data-pid="GDtUEMf6">我：“你不懂，干我们这行的就喜欢认儿子。岁数什么的不重要。”</p>
 <p data-pid="jOtkTIqj">——</p>
 <p data-pid="K0SlaUrw">季晏：唔唔唔</p>
 <p data-pid="ITCKfU0d">——</p>
 <p data-pid="gMfXXgA6">我松开了捂他嘴的手。</p>
 <p data-pid="zL9Kr8y7">——</p>
 <p data-pid="A6NJg12b">季晏怒气冲冲地瞪我：“谁是你儿子！”</p>
 <p data-pid="IMa0ChDT">——</p>
 <p data-pid="nGOupM7G">我：？</p>
 <p data-pid="gJqzrT-r">你怎么回事？</p>
 <p data-pid="TH12hK6H">这都不上道的？</p>
 <p data-pid="oMooc5cW">——</p>
 <p data-pid="Hn_vkLwV">两道目光齐刷刷地看我，</p>
 <p data-pid="mldl-YbE">压力好大。</p>
 <p data-pid="CpqGYJES">——</p>
 <p data-pid="AmEp_kiP">行叭，</p>
 <p data-pid="snooG9ci">我摊了摊手，</p>
 <p data-pid="_l3NgQw9">对太傅说：</p>
 <p data-pid="QTc6dE_e">“好吧。</p>
 <p data-pid="OIagD9wa">其实，</p>
 <p data-pid="NXdyZ_ri">他，季晏，我孙子。”</p>
 <p data-pid="z4-OaPhg">——</p>
 <p data-pid="z97AWfHG">太傅：？</p>
 <p data-pid="iBgLeZjz">季晏：？</p>
 <p data-pid="WWFeR0SC">——</p>
 <p data-pid="-83t2O29">开玩笑的，</p>
 <p data-pid="TLI6dupC">不会真有人信吧？</p>
 <p data-pid="tsDHhca1">——</p>
 <p data-pid="tv_BmfVP">季晏被我气跑了。</p>
 <p data-pid="Axb6u-FH">——</p>
 <p data-pid="-z5g7HaX">哟呼，</p>
 <p data-pid="y62NQTir">脾气还挺大的。</p>
 <p data-pid="DijlEq0V">——</p>
 <p data-pid="6yrk-XfO">带太傅客堂去喝茶，</p>
 <p data-pid="qVxx4m2t">喝了茶总该走了吧。</p>
 <p data-pid="qPTw7LQ4">——</p>
 <p data-pid="oFcqIIS1">太傅上马车前，</p>
 <p data-pid="VC-keAmT">幽幽对我说了一句：</p>
 <p data-pid="e8w1YACw">“贵府的面首，气性不佳，姿色尔尔。”</p>
 <p data-pid="B06SR_Xj">——</p>
 <p data-pid="-W8JdEuA">？</p>
 <p data-pid="JfkQAEuZ">太傅看出季晏是男宠不稀奇，</p>
 <p data-pid="8xdPb6QP">谁不知我钱绥男宠三千，</p>
 <p data-pid="WxM9yFHC">但要说姿色尔尔，</p>
 <p data-pid="_OF2IsRg">这也太挑了吧？</p>
 <p data-pid="ateO36vl">——</p>
 <p data-pid="NvyVJd1n">我回太傅一个眼神：</p>
 <p data-pid="LwCNh_Rs">你美你美你最美，</p>
 <p data-pid="1nAeGP1o">美羊羊都没你美。</p>
 <p data-pid="BTZurkEE">——</p>
 <p data-pid="c3iktx66">太傅：钱绥眼抽筋了。</p>
 <p data-pid="l_zESsTH">——</p>
 <h2>8月3</h2>
 <h3>天凉了，</h3>
 <p data-pid="eeBJBSbM">该解散后院了。</p>
 <p data-pid="LWProp_5">——</p>
 <p data-pid="e-_rvN4y">这天，</p>
 <p data-pid="6qKaF9Vi">我强行召集了后院的三千男宠。</p>
 <p data-pid="3_zRgavk">——</p>
 <p data-pid="VUL8pi0R">到场的只有季晏和容玦。</p>
 <p data-pid="9iJWG-1x">——</p>
 <p data-pid="hTr388P4">？</p>
 <p data-pid="vmrpjLbl">怎么回事？</p>
 <p data-pid="5ZVLk566">其他人当我的话是耳边风吗？</p>
 <p data-pid="IxCnr3Pe">我要生气了。</p>
 <p data-pid="ZjJ9Ea75">——</p>
 <p data-pid="Dp72-l5x">问侍从：</p>
 <p data-pid="TZLhArXD">“其他人呢？”</p>
 <p data-pid="FlAcGi97">——</p>
 <p data-pid="aOHJcc8i">侍从：黄豆流汗.jpg</p>
 <p data-pid="BhLDgPeb">“......大人，您忘了吗，府里头只有两位公子。”</p>
 <p data-pid="GiMqIN5Q">——</p>
 <p data-pid="WuvC3zlV">我：？！</p>
 <p data-pid="kISF7AfW">瞳孔地震</p>
 <p data-pid="Ii5xLfby">这......连三个都没有......</p>
 <p data-pid="y74YlRb-">上次参我本子的御史，</p>
 <p data-pid="zOABomlG">你写三千男宠的时候良心不会痛吗？！</p>
 <p data-pid="DLxi3T9d">——</p>
 <p data-pid="0TU287gk">季晏：“其他人？怎么，你还有其他人？”</p>
 <p data-pid="sd_L0YCU">容玦：...</p>
 <p data-pid="AeQSKOIg">——</p>
 <p data-pid="ZFRM8Dt2">咳咳，</p>
 <p data-pid="4BpvbCSt">我咳了下。</p>
 <p data-pid="s5rxeDQX">“瞎说啥？我又不是那种荒淫无度的人。</p>
 <p data-pid="wNiDZETO">其实今天我找你俩是有重要的事。”</p>
 <p data-pid="OJCljQ_n">——</p>
 <p data-pid="EQD3-aXd">我看了眼天，继续说，</p>
 <p data-pid="upauQdmY">“我看今天天气不错，要不......你俩别干了。”</p>
 <p data-pid="5VDsr9rB">——</p>
 <p data-pid="bK1vmjZA">…</p>
 <p data-pid="B8ocJRDS">感觉气氛有点安静过头了。</p>
 <p data-pid="OEYJd_Sb">——</p>
 <p data-pid="aJVgluK9">容玦脸色白了。</p>
 <p data-pid="cXgZarCe">——</p>
 <p data-pid="KHkX2YJU">季晏突然拽住我的手腕，恶狠狠问：</p>
 <p data-pid="g0vDtPbQ">？！</p>
 <p data-pid="SonUOPSs">“你要始乱终弃？是不是白莲那小......”</p>
 <p data-pid="wcs7nEgo">——</p>
 <p data-pid="syjiPp57">他还没说完，</p>
 <p data-pid="zV4XivZU">变故突生。</p>
 <p data-pid="yFf_HW7a">容玦晕倒了。</p>
 <p data-pid="uxfXRYl7">——</p>
 <p data-pid="NZdfPLu5">季晏：“容玦——”</p>
 <p data-pid="InupuB7T">——</p>
 <p data-pid="zVjjSQjD">！</p>
 <p data-pid="yh_va5aA">我上前揽住倒下的容玦。</p>
 <p data-pid="SaW3a6EV">——</p>
 <p data-pid="kAV2kbv9">怎么办怎么办怎么办</p>
 <p data-pid="h9J0z3ED">对了，</p>
 <p data-pid="B2I38hHY">掐人中！</p>
 <p data-pid="UnNiuWZm">——</p>
 <p data-pid="vV_tSVkI">我——掐！</p>
 <p data-pid="ll3VW0ir">怎么还不醒？</p>
 <p data-pid="dfSOUT8M">再使点劲——</p>
 <p data-pid="fuBfoygm">——</p>
 <p data-pid="ddKjk6wk">侍从：！</p>
 <p data-pid="Hh_eB4VN">“大人，你不要掐了！再掐容公子就要过去了！”</p>
 <p data-pid="_y4jMuT9">——</p>
 <p data-pid="5SAU6wsb">......</p>
 <p data-pid="Hif-UuI3">赵太医来时，</p>
 <p data-pid="joQyZ4T5">看到床上昏迷的容玦，</p>
 <p data-pid="7IVBlqh2">陷入了沉思。</p>
 <p data-pid="VDRoktVB">“容公子这是......被人打了一拳水沟穴？”</p>
 <p data-pid="iugOSbDe">——</p>
 <p data-pid="dwLvD0ym">看一眼容玦肿起的上唇和人中，</p>
 <p data-pid="teBH526C">我心虚地戳了戳手指。</p>
 <p data-pid="I9NziVVn">“算是吧，我掐的。”</p>
 <p data-pid="fp0uh-w-">——</p>
 <p data-pid="cPCEdxUy">赵太医：？</p>
 <p data-pid="0v2IJOob">——</p>
 <p data-pid="pRKhd4tF">赵太医给容玦看病。</p>
 <p data-pid="ex0_vKaL">——</p>
 <p data-pid="2qkO4Gro">看完了。</p>
 <p data-pid="qtTXtaCf">——</p>
 <p data-pid="-7fK8hIp">……</p>
 <p data-pid="En3FxpgS">“容公子体弱，气急攻心，乃至昏厥，并无大碍。平日里多加调理，勿劳神动气……”</p>
 <p data-pid="M0Mgm2jo">赵太医顿了顿，看了一下容玦的嘴，又说，</p>
 <p data-pid="PbRlWkqA">“房事也不宜过于激烈……”</p>
 <p data-pid="MtnRFI0x">——</p>
 <p data-pid="kkNQwql2">我：！</p>
 <p data-pid="p5EbsBA2">住嘴啊你！</p>
 <p data-pid="B9EOBj8v">都说是掐的了！</p>
 <p data-pid="qjz4QB3e">——</p>
 <p data-pid="kDGvfMtf">赵太医走了。</p>
 <p data-pid="m7oA5H5p">——</p>
 <p data-pid="5lSY_kt4">……</p>
 <p data-pid="6fPkhTf5">容玦醒了。</p>
 <p data-pid="IlJJRARj">他迷迷糊糊地睁开眼，</p>
 <p data-pid="EVcKOCiU">看见床头似有人影在晃动。</p>
 <p data-pid="I4p4WQAa">视线里的人影一点一点从模糊到清晰，</p>
 <p data-pid="hf8lLwhT">是钱绥。</p>
 <p data-pid="FzYhC2jR">——</p>
 <p data-pid="8SwTqk1f">“你醒了！”</p>
 <p data-pid="hFfWmyPp">我把碗捧起来，舀了一匙药送到他唇边。</p>
 <p data-pid="Q72QmGNC">“大郎……啊，不。容玦，你该喝药了。”</p>
 <p data-pid="Sb_lwNRZ">——</p>
 <p data-pid="G-S1yOEU">容玦：…</p>
 <p data-pid="4WI34LLu">不太敢喝。</p>
 <p data-pid="1K-8vV7f">——</p>
 <p data-pid="yBN6SYXM">容玦迟迟不张口，</p>
 <p data-pid="_W0Sr3yV">我想了想，说：</p>
 <p data-pid="uzzDrtO4">“放心，不是我熬的。”</p>
 <p data-pid="RRCzskKD">——</p>
 <p data-pid="nvP9kpUr">嗯？</p>
 <p data-pid="8L6i-_sI">他喝了，</p>
 <p data-pid="eiFh9Di3">他竟然喝了？</p>
 <p data-pid="ScDf10xx">哼，我熬的怎么了，不能喝吗？</p>
 <p data-pid="lCxRXwYb">——</p>
 <p data-pid="G-PFoKNy">……</p>
 <p data-pid="HvGeHLhu">思来想去，</p>
 <p data-pid="iQKIPMuQ">我悟了。</p>
 <p data-pid="ZBwtePk4">季晏和容玦这种貌美如花的小公子离了钱府也不知道有什么去处。</p>
 <p data-pid="RQRb0N6T">季晏还能去当个保镖啥的，</p>
 <p data-pid="az9vjIdt">容玦……可能会被掳去当哪个山头的压寨夫人。</p>
 <p data-pid="Vrn_AP9V">——</p>
 <p data-pid="HUgjr6-A">想到了个两全之策。</p>
 <p data-pid="zpljJIyU">——</p>
 <p data-pid="FB9H_NWa">叫来季晏，</p>
 <p data-pid="PHC_gMkw">一起去容玦房间。</p>
 <p data-pid="5he7hVw6">——</p>
 <p data-pid="4eVtGUo8">我左手牵季晏的手，</p>
 <p data-pid="KdOOUYDU">右手牵容玦的手，</p>
 <p data-pid="I_MZnm3x">把他俩的手搭在一起。</p>
 <p data-pid="NoUByC7O">“我决定了，我不能拆散这个家。</p>
 <p data-pid="ep0aS4IR">所以……</p>
 <p data-pid="MXXXqVjA">我们拜把子吧！”</p>
 <p data-pid="Y1b8LFaH">——</p>
 <p data-pid="gkK52--Q">季晏：？</p>
 <p data-pid="f6au-2G7">容玦：？</p>
 <p data-pid="dYWm7o-Q">——</p>
 <p data-pid="OrHvkRbR">不说话就是答应了！</p>
 <p data-pid="s8SfYJRu">——</p>
 <p data-pid="u_-Ufqgt">……</p>
 <p data-pid="fnlVJYGD">好耶，</p>
 <p data-pid="ZkCj-Gu9">成功了！</p>
 <p data-pid="kG8Fjcsg">——</p>
 <p data-pid="bPQnpZ4h">今天起，</p>
 <p data-pid="QxEGbVWj">我是他们大哥了！</p>
 <p data-pid="WPPmmZZo">——</p>
 <p data-pid="wUcCy2ne">突然想起个问题，</p>
 <p data-pid="LLx1_0Ry">“容玦、季晏，</p>
 <p data-pid="8Sg4MpAH">你们当初是怎么入钱府的？”</p>
 <p data-pid="i18Xhu_P">——</p>
 <p data-pid="6arLegR6">季晏嘴角抽了抽，</p>
 <p data-pid="hBJBqCXg">半晌才幽幽道：</p>
 <p data-pid="iY1uyqmY">“你又忘了……</p>
 <p data-pid="MUJMkipk">我们是你掳来的。”</p>
 <p data-pid="nIHbbKfX">——</p>
 <p data-pid="U1y2-1Lu">我：什么？</p>
 <p data-pid="yxj_HpZc">土匪竟是我自己？！</p>
 <p data-pid="eZfJyZXe">——</p>
 <p data-pid="yuDNlMC2">……</p>
 <p data-pid="ST7egTAo">拜把子之后，</p>
 <p data-pid="CbjHH1yG">好像哪里变了，</p>
 <p data-pid="pvCVEfSD">好像又没变。</p>
 <p data-pid="p0I1Gp0F">——</p>
 <p data-pid="vwFmydR-">比如，现在。</p>
 <p data-pid="_9gCBIXp">我躺在床上，</p>
 <p data-pid="i1XQKfiQ">皱着眉头盯着床幔看了一会儿。</p>
 <p data-pid="vWl1pSrm">——</p>
 <p data-pid="XOZZXgk1">憋不住了。</p>
 <p data-pid="coik5Q5S">——</p>
 <p data-pid="myFWuTPz">我侧身问躺在旁边的人：</p>
 <p data-pid="4W4gu206">“为啥你要睡我的床？”</p>
 <p data-pid="OoPNJt-r">——</p>
 <p data-pid="m-f725a0">容玦闭着眼，眼睫纤长细密。</p>
 <p data-pid="ddSAnjsD">他的睡相很端庄，平躺着，</p>
 <p data-pid="ijAzhEnb">双手规规矩矩地交叉放在小腹上。</p>
 <p data-pid="YYziQ7V2">听见我问，好一会才动了动唇：</p>
 <p data-pid="YN0_KISZ">“兄友弟恭，同榻而眠，有何不可？”</p>
 <p data-pid="deRnLUQ6">——</p>
 <p data-pid="S5hjWnHG">我：…</p>
 <p data-pid="KptQempR">但是天气凉了，</p>
 <p data-pid="haM7Sj0b">你有点冻人。</p>
 <p data-pid="cLJVRN0n">——</p>
 <p data-pid="dgTmjWes">我翻了个身，</p>
 <p data-pid="YVMZOhdG">侧到另一边。</p>
 <p data-pid="5EeGWUR1">问躺在我另一侧的人，</p>
 <p data-pid="Mm2mts1r">“你呢？之前不是死活不让我睡你床？”</p>
 <p data-pid="rNyDSVez">——</p>
 <p data-pid="Em_r9FyL">季晏：…</p>
 <p data-pid="WqkptvBM">“你管我！……他睡得，我睡不得吗？食不言寝不语，你哪来这么多话！”</p>
 <p data-pid="lhLsBVVH">——</p>
 <p data-pid="i5ez2yrC">我：…</p>
 <p data-pid="bjuUFggP">不要把话说得这么奇怪啦。</p>
 <p data-pid="n3izK4S4">——</p>
 <p data-pid="Y6KartiV">行叭，</p>
 <p data-pid="fvnV06m1">闭眼，</p>
 <p data-pid="bCDFr64y">睡觉。</p>
 <p data-pid="9lH068oV">——</p>
 <p data-pid="5mn0qyCA">o(—﹏—)o</p>
 <p data-pid="9lGENGvL">床有点挤。</p>
 <p data-pid="Bs5wfo7x">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>8月5</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>早上，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7nMdd3Xd">我是在美人榻上醒来的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r9cdRuXn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U7at0L_W">扭扭脖子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r7GuaOcx">咔咔响。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nagZ6JYN">酸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MZEG-_AK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VooHQNGs">昨天晚上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z4-x2UCJ">也不知道咋回事，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mPsFmRsK">我一左一右的两人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9DuUuhKO">越睡越往中间。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OfjXc9CB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qQDtDosA">季晏像个螃蟹一样，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pzEDdAYR">闭着眼手脚并用，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9QiF4Nav">一点一点向床中间爬。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LonrvUON">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pQw7UMMY">容玦就更神奇了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PNGvA7L1">他保持着端庄的睡姿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p6IZ0sbO">逐渐往中间平移！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TEhJtqby">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GUhuyrG1">我被挤得没地方睡了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sZcy-E-e">于是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WZUVxtL1">一个移形换影技能，</p>
 <p data-pid="2agYgXsE">转移到了美人榻上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oERgcbTa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R5zO4d_C">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ThFXhoML">伸个懒腰，打个哈欠</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="co1PFvJ7">走到床边，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9Fk5x00t">看着熟睡中抱成一团的二人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aYkY5xtJ">我陷入了沉思。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bPjaBqNl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OdgXOXP8">未曾设想的道路增加了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZqlZq0by">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tHg6MDd7">原来…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="50BQigwB">是他们两个想一起睡，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DcOB0meE">又不好意思说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vymwA8bP">拿我当幌子！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CEoKnTLM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q9jUFC-2">灯泡竟是我自己！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bYb9bv_0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2ilQUbFn">还能说什么，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MxQAOquo">祝99。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ueRVu_ug">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7W6iFLws">蹑手蹑脚地开门走了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="94KW2Meq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AbBfknIW">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="F2_DbQ8c">上班。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dNZYlxhM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gDuGOWSx">下班。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9Src6pX_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tQ2GeW5W">回府。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cwHcnih-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q3j_18Qa">发现容玦脸色很臭，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DiXhBkbB">季晏脸上多了个巴掌印。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UXeTVQj6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G7ZbGsWG">晚上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3ZGiQdi8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MOM466wh">看着出现在房间的一红一白两尊大佛，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QYal16Qb">无语子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vcCF-rBV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wv6TJgto">“哈哈哈，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VZHQOCOT">突然想起还有奏折没批，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rFG8Doap">…我去书房。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pz7qSKLg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4GjGjUu3">火速关上门，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5YkCUXR9">溜了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4ICdokiI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nXSjDfB2">书房。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kKogSfLf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Sn_dOLBu">白莲一边磨墨，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HLOBJMcU">一边释放绿茶技能。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QLWpmKVh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CqX1itkN">“季公子容公子真不会心疼人~</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N4YaZfz_">大人今夜去奴家房里歇息吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l3RGh4A0">奴家的床……还蛮大的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Eo11wAeq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ka84XQhQ">我：…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qp5zcYHp">救命，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h0V1oHvh">绿茶味太冲了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kLINNl87">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZG3_tAKX">我把杯子塞到白莲手里，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="psHWk8o8">说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VY99WIDA">“帮我泡一杯普洱茶吧，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iXFcxOxc">最近绿茶喝腻了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vTeyx8QE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8e0UMlC4">白莲：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LoObcNEH">可是你最近喝的是乌龙茶啊。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UJ-FP5FK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ixowTKNh">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nIqA2bXW">把绿茶，啊不，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e2GBc2T-">把白莲打发走了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ecxwGMc_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nrXfnlMq">我一个反手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0GbtDxeH">就把书房给反锁了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4FLUfgZ8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ylbOAajE">清净了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mIP_TVB2">睡觉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6HEzN1qy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HQkfKcQZ">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XOUG7rw6">在书房睡不好，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yBImZ6XQ">熊猫眼再现。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r4Elk1Qz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HvHIPTqI">早朝，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UYJzDXpQ">打瞌睡。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gAtB9n0F">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qBv1aE55">下朝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CcqiPQ5n">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mDzzVpu2">胡岩扯我到角落，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7PHA9u7e">鬼鬼祟祟地问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bFvDRdF3">“钱大人……可是得了阳虚之症？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g_7c3Gsb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ad4_fOwm">我特么…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-IbCSk3a">你特么…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vEKKK7EO">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YSntGXPy">为谢谢他的关心，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WbBnOTdK">我礼貌地问候道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5gTlalfD">“你最近是不是日子过太好了？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QPBZjUAv">想找点刺激？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tm3HcdQ7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GuA-r-GZ">！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2XhMUPFZ">胡岩一个条件反射，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tmieWmTL">后退，弯腰，低头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="68eNAn-L">“不是！臣的意思是……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HUA5np2H">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rcoEP8bp">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W_MKPnya">我一定是脑子进水了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YteLdfGu">不然，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gR0iq3Fd">为什么要跟胡岩去找他师父治肾虚？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R-wjNl7K">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j-lF2Z9j">我根本就没肾虚！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8lpMTwQ1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lf3ElXT5">话说太监会肾虚吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SYoDqHUv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EaZWT26n">胡岩走在前头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HoDEPYbE">语气十分自豪地说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9zplyFOJ">“钱大人，你有所不知。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DY4bBfgO">我师父是整个天朝最神机妙算料事如神足智多谋能掐会算……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nNgx0ebj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kyPy9O93">我：…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uVPRwKLk">这么多唯物论知识，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0NrEqFOO">感觉白教他了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T6kosehW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZWxGC3nt">我拎起胡岩，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZQ3VFY5O">问他：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CYPOXPO8">“你那神机妙算的师父，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VqxZaTVQ">有算到你即将会被我打一顿吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NGaKh1-B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cs6nar4d">胡岩：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tsLXnoeb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SyBQAPX3">不至于吧，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2ccLkOtN">稍微吓唬一下，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VlQiBDmz">就抖成这样。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="485Z54K-">没意思。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CD3hB7NI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NiR9Qmq5">我把人放下来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4BJNCDCQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PL2Ls_Et">“啧，带路。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NbNuc5M6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-JoiefGC">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZYcywKTd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Th9wqxGH">开始怀疑胡岩在耍我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0RjKk9YV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l6IPlxFO">皇宫里还有这种的地方？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hlKiUUY3">这……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="71XrcVxE">破破烂烂的小木屋。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XM8rlSNT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h9GK_49k">进屋。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_DdFeqLl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YI0ZjlEk">胡岩毕恭毕敬喊道：“师父。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dm9UXxVo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6HWWJklL">他的师父背对着我们，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3jh0lQPU">披头散发，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GGIpHIob">一副世外高人的样子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M_g_eR4O">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7aacNt7K">这可怜的老头儿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-Aqvgx0e">一把年纪，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3pRoUP7O">头发都全白了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3GIXZMZR">还要出来装神弄鬼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0FmHc2Vh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="chcw4eJG">不过仔细看看老头还挺高的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d0Ww519W">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fpaOwYv5">老头转身了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zR2hfwlM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gnbKtklC">！</p>
 <p data-pid="BPr8wPde">！！</p>
 <p data-pid="JzTkC-H5">！！！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2MoW3Jg_">我错了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e4nUC93d">这是白、白、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tE5WG3Zj">白发美人！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hT6YLSt_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jNg8Q0mF">口水不知不觉流了下来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7-cLOIzZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v4m-jzAS">戳了戳胡岩，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8zApUFUN">小声问他：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dMhHpPnn">“你师父今年几岁？有对象了吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3vUtLBZS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LeA8G0RV">白发美人说话了：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EjQZ-qIN">“岩儿先出去吧，我同这位钱大人有话说。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LKlTyJvS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sboYAHHt">美人声音也好好听，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ui-hhNMX">我好爱。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gg47JJ8X">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t5a3alWa">胡岩：“可是，师父……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TSIOmxrR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ieSX0gcO">我抹了把口水，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VWfdsxsM">慈爱地看着胡岩说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RzXK38a4">“没事的，岩儿，听你师父的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AgL3_CnY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q7_AJt8W">胡岩：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QTBhiU5B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B02LHNRl">8月5</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pcXLT3cH">白发美人叫姜殷，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oOiSv79b">是个国师。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QrNF9mX3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NpJ19uhd">说实话，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QoEJ6-yW">我也是第一次知道，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gyVuRkZu">我朝，有国师？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Yn369gNB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Exq24C_o">姜殷啃着鸡腿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Yo95Eg_K">口齿含糊地说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0hR0J5ii">“你不知道正常，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3DkZyzRY">因为知道的……根本就没几个人。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lKXdFwBd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3ZCpoSWn">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SPzAh2HJ">你哪来的鸡腿？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kZwXQEsF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fMONguRy">姜殷眨巴眨巴眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8BlolSqs">雪白的睫毛也跟着颤动，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qa6IJNLN">“看啥？你也想吃啊？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JJ6bWILs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gJn-Wmlv">哼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="osRJMmBp">笑死，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Il1Aciu9">谁会吃这种来历不明的人给的东西？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SkpwpQIs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="niFvtymT">…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-lUFg5Y4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dS6oUWn9">“真香。这鸡腿你做的吗？还有吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S4XT982O">我吐出骨头，擦了擦嘴上的油。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0AFeo6is">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OOiLZiwH">姜殷很高兴的样子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OfbqKUHX">“你也喜欢啊，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="leTG13qg">是我从御膳房偷来的！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DF-uJRU-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wt2oAAhp">我蚌住了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zmW00Zij">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pnr9M4fx">姜殷舔了舔唇，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d5iADsWE">还在兴致勃勃地说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="52JtB8Gk">“御膳房我都吃腻了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OuULb_nt">也不知道宫外的东西滋味如何……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gowzYYKP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XM48K3v-">我算是明白了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T0RIhSY2">姜殷是个笨蛋吃货美人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Dn6U7KQl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uOX8NGw6">但是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OdQcehDx">我不是来找神机妙算的国师的吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZGuhUVar">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xo3Tttv3">我问姜殷：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="57C97DAU">“你……会治肾虚吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="buB6Jy-m">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4G5E5sJ4">姜殷：“不会啊。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jyyvKQUW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SSpkA_zX">“那你算无遗策料事如神吗？”、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iPskIby7">“没有啊。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vysFmIrp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="avkykyqw">怒了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WAUd1Hu5">胡岩你给我等着！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mlAwUsf7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="go_KF_wy">“你让胡岩忽悠我来的？为什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rghED6-_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LiuxL3f0">姜殷笑了：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WkjrnxFo">“你带我出宫玩几天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="spiGgvLn">我就告诉你。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pP3r90lC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1EEfcvrq">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rhNlOn4o">不会吧，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6oWuNZWI">他不知道现在已经不兴这套路了吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DVocp10H">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bAAIy_c8">我笑了笑，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WvbfKo7_">一个转身，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ux4_on0e">走了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3I9rYO_n">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HpjEABSR">淦，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mrruWfd0">走不动。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DhdIdx1d">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7A0E8i0a">“你别走——带我出去嘛带我出去嘛——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LSC-uKk0">姜殷哭唧唧地抱住了我的腿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Az6RUY7R">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u6c8xH9J">我：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cNf27MNE">“不要把你嘴上的油蹭我衣服上！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hZJv1vip">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1thSS979">带姜殷去耍。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kLvS8qoW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OQwe0oUH">我变善良了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9p5PbZpM">要知道，搁以前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="STPSS40q">姜殷这种人是会被我揍成猪头的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n9d5yaV3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FBLhRwXU">京城大街。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j9XNrOAM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Nlb4QtGY">姜殷像个好奇宝宝，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4bcW6WxL">问这问那的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GQfWrFnJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1lYUbwuM">“这是什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jACZ5Bra">“冰糖葫芦。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pEDo_s1I">“那是什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="90rEjscc">“竹蜻蜓。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qo8SFaZo">“他们在干什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fBM_bAOP">“斗蛐蛐。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dTGIUzsr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yi6rlk_x">那边的某个纨绔子弟看斗蛐蛐看得正上头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yKnum9Lo">突然发现，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="F5HQqrbV">自己笼子里的常胜将军不见了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y0jtiOib">“啊！我的常胜将军不见了！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z2BFLcuq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oW9HyDNU">我转身一看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dcWC4O54">发现姜殷手里捏着一只蛐蛐，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8rOqWb2X">正举到眼前细细观察着。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HPgWyBtd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lMCkd5gu">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HTwmpdvU">喂，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="adX1pkk_">你不要偷拿别人的蛐蛐啊！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IdG4pzDm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vc3FA6zl">姜殷见我看他，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_SprJwfh">歪头：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lfzywgV6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YdkyJHq7">住手啊，笨蛋！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EMx1ovbD">你快把它捏死了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HZet_p9d">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xn_dPRVy">被纨绔子弟发现了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2e4ZA-mf">“前面那小子，你敢偷我常胜将军！别跑！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f0TjrQkN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ga1w7Zpw">我扔了一袋银子过去，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QO2qlfVv">抓起姜殷就跑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lHKxabJD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fL02UP5w">那位大兄弟，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U3l1Xj8M">对不住了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KDjDAra5">我会帮你埋了这只蛐蛐的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ntcrp1nP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NyJGTMp3">跑了五条街。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VNtR7U4b">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="v2oUTVZZ">md</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4MX5-CQe">呼——呼——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r_Mas3M7">好累。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LC93AA8B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5fOazsjE">姜殷也气喘吁吁的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OwXwpyay">扶着墙，弯腰咯咯地笑了起来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tFHS2zrS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u6bKAq39">我：…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IIKVxQmw">想打人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sCK_GAcm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Cv-xULV_">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MjZzb3Tk">埋蛐蛐。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V_NR03Ll">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C_6GpLfH">去酒楼吃饭喝酒。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iKyWzfpg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sus6oeNY">钱不够，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YrUqqSk2">让姜殷去后厨洗盘子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cbH3UZEX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tXLrfto9">盘子全砸了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bUW48jV6">又欠了钱。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BCnc7oEP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5nZTnkR6">偶遇太傅，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="An60tdvF">被赎出来了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DrtMkf0l">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rzerthh8">太傅看一眼姜殷，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sQA6jMXK">问我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XdIIIXHZ">“这位是……？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BwNfkxtJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Wm3sHwl5">我：“国师。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6sFvQ-lt">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HKE358WH">太傅挑了挑眉：“哦？我怎的不知本朝有国师？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tab1PSiB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9HgXdXve">姜殷挠头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8J8EgyHS">“哈哈哈没关系，我也不认识你。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ivh82YrU">——</p>
 <p data-pid="VfP6k-aJ">——</p>
 <h2>8月6</h2>
 <h3>太傅盯着姜殷看了好久。</h3>
 <p data-pid="7pZKZC0W">——</p>
 <p data-pid="E1b-ge6s">好久。</p>
 <p data-pid="6Ht86iMg">——</p>
 <p data-pid="yZ_VTIOl">？</p>
 <p data-pid="X9hYbQ-7">他们是看对眼了吗？</p>
 <p data-pid="a5-4ISnB">如果是这样，</p>
 <p data-pid="ZHezpOMG">我也不是不能忍痛割爱……</p>
 <p data-pid="RkXhcSKt">——</p>
 <p data-pid="UtjH1xK3">我还在纠结要不要给他俩牵线搭桥时，</p>
 <p data-pid="MeFCHb6C">太傅收回了看姜殷的视线，</p>
 <p data-pid="D5y-XOp-">慢条斯理地说：</p>
 <p data-pid="DK1wdd4H">“冒充国师招摇撞骗，罪当……”</p>
 <p data-pid="ncqsCnfu">——</p>
 <p data-pid="BuYQai0k">！</p>
 <p data-pid="fvvWuCLF">我拉过姜殷，挡在身后。</p>
 <p data-pid="MjIG4WJ3">——</p>
 <p data-pid="SA4MXIn9">“……哈哈哈，刚刚没说清楚。</p>
 <p data-pid="nwXrR66L">这个笨蛋姓姜名殷，字国师，你可以叫他小国或者小师。”</p>
 <p data-pid="rwEE6cNQ">——</p>
 <p data-pid="mTgHjGXP">太傅挑了嘴角，笑着说：</p>
 <p data-pid="v0f-GR_1">“原来如此。”</p>
 <p data-pid="BQwFNEJF">——</p>
 <p data-pid="sL8P0l9w">姜殷从我身后探出脑袋，</p>
 <p data-pid="ZAUiI8Ga">说：</p>
 <p data-pid="tq50yGdF">“不是啊，我就是国……</p>
 <p data-pid="rq5L0-dM">啊，好疼！钱绥你干嘛踩我！”</p>
 <p data-pid="MTDqtZjs">——</p>
 <p data-pid="azsRKEtB">我回头对姜殷扯出一个笑，</p>
 <p data-pid="ssJayWFz">“刚刚看见你脚上有小强。”</p>
 <p data-pid="548cdrKl">——</p>
 <p data-pid="myOq7HWr">拖着姜殷走了。</p>
 <p data-pid="RRESGwE1">——</p>
 <p data-pid="PrUnrUZg">……</p>
 <p data-pid="P6UbXSOf">“钱绥钱绥，小强是什么？”</p>
 <p data-pid="an7grdYV">“蜚蠊。”</p>
 <p data-pid="G3Dzgcda">“为什么叫小强？”</p>
 <p data-pid="OihaMnbH">“闭嘴。”</p>
 <p data-pid="EqT7V-fo">……</p>
 <p data-pid="Fpzh11W0">——</p>
 <p data-pid="RX0ZeO67">……</p>
 <p data-pid="ywr1-DKC">太傅站在原地，</p>
 <p data-pid="fiO0DR97">看着钱绥拉着那白发少年渐行渐远。</p>
 <p data-pid="WRh0jQse">——</p>
 <p data-pid="NYOmMAJ1">……</p>
 <p data-pid="5C3eFxhQ">呃，</p>
 <p data-pid="BsXvVvk0">钱绥又走回来了。</p>
 <p data-pid="M2dd-_By">——</p>
 <p data-pid="2x7AjsOh">……</p>
 <p data-pid="ItKc_k6y">走着，</p>
 <p data-pid="vaOI2spL">我一拍脑袋，想起来，</p>
 <p data-pid="gkh9FrS2">差点忘了太傅。</p>
 <p data-pid="pRVnQndp">还没还人家钱呢。</p>
 <p data-pid="cPBVSRoN">——</p>
 <p data-pid="w8VbXMru">回头拉了太傅一起走。</p>
 <p data-pid="0AaA2ag8">——</p>
 <p data-pid="WQab-q7H">感觉好奇怪啊，</p>
 <p data-pid="47ngHB36">左手拉一个，</p>
 <p data-pid="o_h75LBN">右手拉一个。</p>
 <p data-pid="YNi15Oi1">——</p>
 <p data-pid="XbFzCvBA">突然想起一首歌，</p>
 <p data-pid="Y0Krgsic">左手~一只鸡~</p>
 <p data-pid="Y72JtVqK">右手~一只鸭~</p>
 <p data-pid="9u5UP6Eg">——</p>
 <p data-pid="aKdlv8tt">对不起，</p>
 <p data-pid="phk6jkfC">噗哈哈哈哈哈哈</p>
 <p data-pid="XjZ2nyuG">——</p>
 <p data-pid="49fMi__t">……</p>
 <p data-pid="BGywUgTc">——</p>
 <p data-pid="YyOReOia">回府拿钱。</p>
 <p data-pid="swXoxVG2">——</p>
 <p data-pid="kle5FUJ3">还钱给太傅。</p>
 <p data-pid="EwUaupDN">——</p>
 <p data-pid="sFgruyGq">送太傅回府。</p>
 <p data-pid="sABpTS2L">——</p>
 <p data-pid="62acVBuW">送姜殷回皇宫小破木屋。</p>
 <p data-pid="T_fubN3h">——</p>
 <p data-pid="HULFa9I9">走之前，</p>
 <p data-pid="58GEKZ-i">姜殷扒着门框可怜兮兮地看我：</p>
 <p data-pid="m379P8oQ">“钱绥，明天记得来找我玩啊。”</p>
 <p data-pid="FMNUzy72">——</p>
 <p data-pid="GLsfJeuL">我：…</p>
 <p data-pid="o-B5tPWy">上班，没空。</p>
 <p data-pid="VBSbCtaQ">今天已经划水一天了。</p>
 <p data-pid="-5od8Ioi">——</p>
 <p data-pid="Mw4V4eHO">“后天呢？”</p>
 <p data-pid="lr98oFsm">“上班。”</p>
 <p data-pid="JTnzfenn">“大后天？”</p>
 <p data-pid="IoBHJ9m3">“……”</p>
 <p data-pid="PVuBZGem">——</p>
 <p data-pid="ZAg2_82P">我：…</p>
 <p data-pid="q0F1UEy6">想了想，</p>
 <p data-pid="F4wXf8e5">我留下了一句万能话术。</p>
 <p data-pid="Glcy0l8W">“下次一定。”</p>
 <p data-pid="_RwWbjZo">——</p>
 <p data-pid="zL3ivIQO">……</p>
 <p data-pid="VWwaChGW">——</p>
 <p data-pid="l-IKZdhi">最近又忙了起来，</p>
 <p data-pid="1u-LAjV7">社畜在哪都是社畜啊。</p>
 <p data-pid="sNRxMg9y">——</p>
 <p data-pid="VyoJBZcO">……</p>
 <p data-pid="29lUwYZq">上班，</p>
 <p data-pid="juEWYIHC">和一群老头吵架。</p>
 <p data-pid="9KX0V_wA">下班。</p>
 <p data-pid="XZpmkcs6">……</p>
 <p data-pid="RZ-YTZ0v">——</p>
 <p data-pid="9FcRSqgZ">回府也没能歇着。</p>
 <p data-pid="U3AFwUd1">——</p>
 <p data-pid="QkYlxLwL">今天帮小壮找失踪的母鸡，</p>
 <p data-pid="MFnlIicO">明天被季晏拉去比剑，</p>
 <p data-pid="3lQ6cCs2">后天陪容玦下棋，</p>
 <p data-pid="phCnSGIN">大后天品尝白莲泡的新绿茶。</p>
 <p data-pid="vhT5a3qs">……</p>
 <p data-pid="QBL8_XTW">——</p>
 <p data-pid="MXVGF_K3">忙里偷闲，</p>
 <p data-pid="R8hqXogK">带姜殷见识世面。</p>
 <p data-pid="5Ia_6fdj">——</p>
 <p data-pid="vL11CLXs">勾栏瓦肆，秦楼楚馆，啥地方都去</p>
 <p data-pid="BVP-gNsg">斗鸡走狗，花鸟古董，华灯烟火，啥都玩一点</p>
 <p data-pid="90EeBrqH">——</p>
 <p data-pid="I22vBF8l">先声明，</p>
 <p data-pid="xdy2gLn7">是姜殷想玩，</p>
 <p data-pid="Z4VPj5bZ">我只是勉为其难陪同。</p>
 <p data-pid="Wn8RHY1F">——</p>
 <p data-pid="j2Rfvz4c">这天，</p>
 <p data-pid="eEYkexzB">又带姜殷去玩。</p>
 <p data-pid="IWE2thOQ">——</p>
 <p data-pid="8Rf1bvDz">某家不知名但贼好吃的小饭馆里，</p>
 <p data-pid="Q8g_CBHJ">我和姜殷围着一张小桌子吃东西。</p>
 <p data-pid="eLNO02ZT">——</p>
 <p data-pid="hHuZ8-zZ">我耳朵太好使了，</p>
 <p data-pid="MZ73MJBb">听见掌柜大娘在窃窃私语：</p>
 <p data-pid="_eCBtDLQ">“就是那桌，那个俊小伙儿和头戴幂篱的小娘子……”</p>
 <p data-pid="_wW6CY_k">——</p>
 <p data-pid="W1513tPI">……</p>
 <p data-pid="SdH8X4Um">我看了一眼头戴幂篱的小娘子——</p>
