 <p data-pid="1-OKeQwD">姜殷。</p>
 <p data-pid="j_VO_2Hn">——</p>
 <p data-pid="_5mXDttG">他白头发太扎眼了，</p>
 <p data-pid="C5kwgsRA">平时出门，</p>
 <p data-pid="OiANqa7c">我都找个幂篱给他盖上。</p>
 <p data-pid="-C9XPLxX">——</p>
 <p data-pid="armtZaHZ">？</p>
 <p data-pid="3sInXkUr">掌柜眼睛是不是不好使啊？</p>
 <p data-pid="SbzMyjO8">谁见过长这么高的小娘子？</p>
 <p data-pid="lClvgN_2">——</p>
 <p data-pid="Q1WgNmqS">掌柜大娘又在说了，</p>
 <p data-pid="dzFcY0_5">“……啧啧，我就说，越俊的男人越花心……</p>
 <p data-pid="Wi-ZzHPG">昨日他们两个走后，那俊小伙的夫人带着侍从来问我……</p>
 <p data-pid="HzDqBkC4">我才知这人整日不粘家……竟是养了外室……可怜那貌美如花的夫人……”</p>
 <p data-pid="wvk5a1A_">——</p>
 <p data-pid="2qgsM6Gr">我：…？</p>
 <p data-pid="Jtb-jDmT">乱说什么玩意？</p>
 <p data-pid="8vaTFvPB">——</p>
 <p data-pid="QkLGuH2p">姜殷没有听见掌柜大娘的窃窃私语，</p>
 <p data-pid="vYw7RFWv">他嘴里叼着面，</p>
 <p data-pid="PHKzmG-1">抬眼看我：</p>
 <p data-pid="U7qTeHTC">“钱绥，你怎么不吃啊？”</p>
 <p data-pid="D552T_fu">——</p>
 <p data-pid="2kdS_mvx">我：…</p>
 <p data-pid="GgWRrm02">听到自己的八卦，</p>
 <p data-pid="beNbgoba">有点吃不下。</p>
 <p data-pid="jeOCVAiu">——</p>
 <p data-pid="Kc-iVXm4">想拉人走了。</p>
 <p data-pid="9dAygsYo">——</p>
 <p data-pid="skZYi5-C">我喊道：</p>
 <p data-pid="9brzi9KC">“掌柜的，结——”</p>
 <p data-pid="OQv4NKyb">——</p>
 <p data-pid="Sc12ATdO">不远处传来的一声高呼盖过了我的声音。</p>
 <p data-pid="gFLPmOid">“钱绥——你竟真的在外面有人了！”</p>
 <p data-pid="VB25-ZBc">——</p>
 <p data-pid="MZNBCkRr">这熟悉的声音——</p>
 <p data-pid="4kNGPghL">我扭头看去：？</p>
 <p data-pid="96plmHKB">季晏？白莲？</p>
 <p data-pid="ruy6ZXlA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>8月8</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>爷傻了，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A6ry9pU0">饭馆里的人齐刷刷地扭头看我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H-2Ihua4">全在等着吃瓜。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zbVUgGAN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M_fxEd_7">掌柜大娘：指指点点.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="116QdEwW">“瞧瞧，这不捉奸来了……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LCUVI8tc">这就是到处沾花惹草的下场……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cgMmMD4Z">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xcon4qCq">我：…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OfpfHEDz">QAQ</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7Av3hFBd">我不是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WMRFxMpP">我没有，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O6VD0G5j">别瞎说。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_o87QzUm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1J8F3mwP">我看了看还在吸溜面条的姜殷，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DNlk2lHn">还有气势汹汹的白莲季晏二人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dILj1KzG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D1cCD0FU">权衡利弊之下，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gm_iEd1y">我果断地，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bQBwvHFk">拉起姜殷就跑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UfDQ89f0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qURV7IUZ">姜殷措不及防被面条糊了一脸，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OqNU2xfh">又在疾跑之中灌了一嘴风，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MlJaTb8o">“啊啊啊跑什么啊——钱绥——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lS4YYr6D">我的面——还没吃完——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ieQv-fRX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sMh9KUdl">我一个暴栗过去，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y4VI1nJQ">“就知道吃！逃命啦！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aLmO77f0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xDl7fjz7">回头一看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z7r2kBHT">季晏跟在身后穷追不舍，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hR-r-4R6">还在吼我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iDpZ7rLx">“钱绥！你——又——跑——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1vrZ73BH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xfyt4SkH">我不跑等着你来抓吗！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7yDMO8i7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l0IZwktx">一路狂奔，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o9bbvOiu">撞翻了三个水果摊，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="91mUBeFR">踩破了四家瓦顶，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z3KsJTr-">吓哭了五个小孩，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yCPld18e">收到了很多声问候——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lSUrxZhU">“哪家的混小子？赶着投胎哪？赔钱——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="34f2OZxp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8izEgCjy">跑到死胡同了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="axBrOkhY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rDwaKAot">…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3WTYegZH">天要亡我！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-qF5Ujf8">我松开了姜殷的手。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CB8xa5sK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ARnZ3HPq">姜殷累得一下子瘫坐在地上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ydU8t5YQ">却突然拉住我的手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ef2Ef0Am">兴奋地说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UxrHV1tM">“好、好玩！我们继续跑吧！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2i609kUs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hlGkpXm-">我：…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0i40KW2Z">憨批欢乐多。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pKUH3bKk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lXB2g4FE">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TEibWy6T">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vzxnZnG2">被季晏逮着了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jSe9dnun">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TMb67tT_">被提溜回府。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5mZqLX8C">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W2_8BfEw">接受三庭会审。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K1U-GSH_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="laPkJsFd">我和姜殷站在大堂中间。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3cAQUoSh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZSYd6Qg7">容玦冷着脸，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xm-M30qr">季晏臭着脸，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FF0KvALS">白莲捂着脸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tNPqN0tN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JlRMbNjl">我：…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Va8G9p_u">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GekrvOtn">季晏冷笑一声，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AeYNSavK">指着姜殷，问我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gy9rBFAK">“他是谁？才多久，你又认了个好弟弟？看来在外头风流快活得很……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_WeroqmB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i4AvJf-J">容玦抿着嘴不说话。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KrowODZ2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CSmhF5LP">白莲掩面低泣。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ANQd7vec">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Cbc1y4TR">我愣是给这架势整蒙了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wd_J6Gsc">我……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y3DENEZM">我没干啥吧？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ENWQrTkH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lJ59ihFh">姜殷说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BEUwIxIl">“什么弟弟？我不是啊。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TLwhNtqT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lhJaa50k">我疯狂点头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dcTcOxw6">“对对对，不是。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uWFblXce">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ww88-lfB">季晏容玦面色稍缓。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rokjT9ji">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U4UgENWU">姜殷又说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3-9AtroF">“我们只是一起去吃喝玩乐啦，其他什么也来得及没做啊！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MzF1DSjE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z1MiZuBx">我：…？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rNBxbm3C">话是这么说，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MGcZ1Wlk">就……哪里怪怪的？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MW9NJKbc">————</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qivfRXp2">果然，一时间，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tmFkuxdQ">季晏头上都冒火了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i_VUgiqM">揪起姜殷的衣领就要打一顿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="81ZkOhML">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xwBUKgMt">我：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4OJ1FNdw">我冲上前抱住要动手的季晏。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GUr4b1TW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U1XWa2FB">姜殷咻一下跑到我身后。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vTjGiuUY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x9prIW0f">季晏：（╯‵□′）╯.</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2a6rHb7D">“钱绥你还敢护着他！？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S6V9eMGh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZKuCwGBC">姜殷：Σ( ° △ °|||)︴</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="phsh8gBD">“钱绥我好害怕！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lvLKAkUd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gBvKfRto">我：○|￣|_</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ugWziTqL">不要打了不要打了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ufY7_wPF">要打去练舞室打！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7RJoeEIb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nq0WoBCm">看着这混作一团的场面，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1FzCZ1AQ">容玦：......呵。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dTPlvbwm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UnK-DQIM">白莲撕碎了手帕：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jkMdWdWO">这新来的有点东西，竟然茶得浑然天成！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XrjKJ5Fk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h0A_vBM0">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3pu-FZcG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pCw5Cywf">我费劲口舌，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cryrjQAm">他们终于相信，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LXD90U-7">我真的没出去瞎搞。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mh334VHq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UrpOgxzv">摇头叹气，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uGX2QT-W">很纳闷，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bF-ykXtg">我到底是个什么形象在他们眼里？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LXhZ8Si-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JTuuxf9M">不懂。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W7xxal3Q">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WUbkqudW">......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cY4cJgys">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XlkgcuUU">被容玦罚抄清静经。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DjyMmzRd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6onUDbMu">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u18ld_lI">你怎么敢的？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-FM_MK9K">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RTex2TxS">容玦掩着唇，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R_n42Yum">低低咳了几声，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="74e_PAzv">面色好像有些苍白。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zYS_1IHR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ma63fHsA">我：......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D_Lg8-5g">...行叭。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fK4zHss8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2oxj_yWM">抄了三天。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OmIAHBmK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J4_NF4h2">我悟了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CQkJJs0N">感觉自己无欲无求，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M6TsA0jf">即将参悟大道得道成仙。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3ODPkOHb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QOXVDUk7">被抓去加班。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_GViJF2G">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R937m0G7">(ノ｀⊿´)ノ</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oHZ74ALG">成个p仙嘞，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="txIp93bz">起来打工啦！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jSamue2B">——</p>
 <h2>8月9</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>我火急火燎赶到皇宫，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Vd8ctvz0">一个官员没见着。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8xnboHjY">只有一只糯米团子扑了上来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OM1ecSA_">“义父——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o7fwC6Ug">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PjaBRHoi">被扑了满怀，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YJloPHny">小皇帝毛茸茸的头在我怀里乱蹭。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pGqbo73_">我：……？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yA52sSJS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5NxVthDB">想把人扒拉下来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Zcd1V_hU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tfBN7RId">没等我动手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4p1El5PO">一只手从旁边伸出来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a1pItfVw">捏着小皇帝的后脖子把他扯下来了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u8Hzjse4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DRt9rH_Z">我顺着手看过去，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Yvj3cZ1r">啊？太傅在呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-3w0gESz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o7C-M_Fu">小皇帝被提在空中，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hmefmpkO">手舞足蹈的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DL5j4YXb">“老师，快放我下来！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GjX6bSJl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="48dBlZML">太傅长身玉立，巍然不动。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9OIVBNJC">他瞥一眼小皇帝，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JpwLlwrQ">凉凉开口道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VotzNB8X">“规矩呢？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="80T2TLwZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LGkePtkk">小皇帝：…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CszIQPUm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0uB0g_Fp">我看不下去了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_P01XPEn">把小皇帝解救下来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E4PL0tVi">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zlf8x0C6">我左右看了看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pnYkV12s">问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zCE9o4Rm">“不是有加急事件吗？什么事？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N1GTwEEH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sU0hw_8G">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BYTTJcJ7">“这个嘛……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="epar-xpX">小皇帝看向了左边，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J6ZKepKn">太傅看向了右边。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xx6qA4vu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-se8I0bF">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AFyMtkiM">敢情搁这耍我呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VnB76XsP">我要闹了啊。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NL7HP6gf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tRCYfGfD">太傅轻咳了一声，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lRQiREaN">把小皇帝推到我面前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PXfmpfH-">说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qFXnPz28">“陛下近日睡不好。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YHz9di3V">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hRujYIZ1">这……紧急事件？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2eFtBWVp">我：“失眠找赵太医啊。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NRl-7PCU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="55I8OC9d">小皇帝偷偷看一眼太傅，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Mf83mf_K">说：“我不要赵太医</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D-vLRH82">……我要听义父讲故事！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I3Y7gTmM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4Nncp3Ui">这样啊……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_sLUOUCR">突然有些骄傲，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tb5K5M8Q">我讲的故事竟然好到不听睡不着吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I7jH6RL4">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pn8jOSFG">清嗓子，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x2eFt9BE">准备讲故事。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Rr6gOQQS">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BTYKgRkq">然而，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IxJm1Thi">这小东西才爬上床，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HxZGpTLD">三秒后就睡着了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UZXHKJnu">并且开始流哈喇子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7hhVsSR5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n_Oaa8Bz">我：…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="svt0mEBP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0QJmdriJ">爷笑了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tBFF13m3">这叫睡不好吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6FXVIOHw">敢耍我？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Md1sJcJ2">改天我非得揍他一顿不可。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uisnGgw1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aQbY07Dg">叹气，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qov3SRZj">帮小皇帝掖掖被子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fQ5_sTAH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z87NSarP">出门，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aclQ6yHc">准备回府。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="umP-S0VC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ol8R3Wma">咚——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TyIpCyb4">撞到人了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IiL1DrvM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Nv0jdhlZ">我：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VnbNzbIt">吓死我了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0WnwJD3s">太傅你怎么神出鬼没的？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d22W4Wco">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0YhsJ-8L">太傅被我撞得一踉跄，后退了一步。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iFSPL6c1">他站稳后，理了理衣袖。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mQ9_EYyU">说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ikk_xTlr">“莽撞。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Yr7yxAK2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pkK_Znmh">我：…</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ziRYVwib">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ShCpEAal">“太傅，你没事吧？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5tmMV5Q5">“…”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Onhu_bPz">“那我先回去啦。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DV0I-rtM">“慢着。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-uTqmX4s">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bVLEFsRK">“嗯？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u0sXhtOl">我回过头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XiZXK8sg">“咋了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BxnYN1x9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OPYjz-BL">太傅站在月色中，像个玉人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VdkDrIzn">他微垂着眼帘，说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xHS53jFo">“明日是仲秋，夜宴后你……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YUqkqwF3">留在宫里上值。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UvfNXR6m">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lqZD3gja">我：……？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IqNG-Q_M">我裂开了。</p>
 <p data-pid="bKo7O5Bj">——</p>
 <h2>8月10</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>中秋晚上加班？</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TgxJTFWr">求求你做个人吧！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y0VN-rjZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qb-Q19N7">我带着救世的心入宫，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6qJmEIIo">怀着灭世的心出宫。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AbnNkzQV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6b3aCtgT">走到宫门口了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qT0elg4i">我停住了脚步。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MUZeXMt-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BvbIHGa1">想了想，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BkxBsJJN">好几天没找姜殷了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yJM0KxIs">不如顺便去看一下。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="k9ooDlJB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xH1GmNHk">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r_CcmaQO">小破木屋前。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3ogSPG7i">——</p>
 <p data-pid="J0c0wPfs">敲门。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VYFUOzXi">咚咚咚——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FNyQ9Mog">“姜殷姜殷，你睡了吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T-NizJ0c">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q1r-95ah">几乎我话音刚落，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cQputp_n">门啪一声开了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pEJra_Ou">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D-MVBJi0">姜殷顶着一头杂乱的白毛，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Mbu8EYhB">双眼却在放光，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5ng4IheH">兴致冲冲地问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NcpuaQes">“还没睡！钱绥你来找我玩吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f96_wW9P">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zCP5RIHj">看着他充满期盼的眼睛，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HdL63eN3">我也不忍心拒绝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TOJ1NV-O">虽然本来只是想来看看他的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="os8MGNVr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Nan3Cy7b">我：“啊，对。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Sai_1sKm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1Aintk1i">姜殷捋了一下翘起的呆毛，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7oyultWm">扯着我边走边说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kXMLDAbA">“我听说京城夜间的市集可有趣了……还有那个……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xh1Rw5BM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M4n3Uwwz">的确，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="janyFATr">夜间的京城，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G1dqZ1Z3">相比白日别具一番风味。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H0SaeICR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="exDjEkEE">仲秋将至，市集间正悬灯结彩。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RRyHwT7O">夜市千灯照碧云，高楼红袖客纷纷。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vdUOuSex">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xLzcXowV">没错，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZWbNYl4g">我带姜殷来醉花楼了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2UhNcZ-3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CCzqi5F3">“花魁姐姐！我带朋友来了！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VLSIsSk9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Sokg0CCo">花魁正对镜描唇贴翠，熏香敷粉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Zx4sYaH6">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WGm_geDP">她听见钱绥的声音一时喜不自胜，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3_1Hex5i">听清他说又带了人来时，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3lsJm8YZ">突就添了几分恼怒。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Di4xgyMj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_EqkdClj">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qS5KjOap">我推开厢房的门，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Jn0gl8pn">见花魁姐姐背对着我们。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cLNrSlDF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WFS4HejP">？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EvD637Fc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7aUSSsRe">我上前走到她身侧，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OAiQBFme">弯腰附身，轻唤道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HRzbLxNR">“花魁姐姐？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rOZceTr5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W5dOoMDI">花魁把头偏到另一边。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OG_hhNRa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B_yzuaC-">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OfiOAOe5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bkTNAXzE">谁知姜殷这个憨憨学我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ayzj2_KC">走到花魁的另一侧，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="atFcRK_b">弯腰歪头，问：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DXirsYqu">“花魁姐姐？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-ya6Hp_T">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="10888yjE">花魁措不及防，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M1fnKzwQ">被姜殷雪白的脸吓了一跳。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kdrvsDy8">“啊——钱大人！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z3ca9552">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j5ppEFoF">我扶住了险些掉地上的花魁。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8jOBcPd_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PVQMBEiE">我有些抱歉，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jxa0TJCA">“不好意思啊，姐姐。他是我朋友。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X-Z27SIR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CyZOiv7L">花魁回过神来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jn1ZScSG">瞪了姜殷一眼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ro-Ndhzh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4Awv1GEC">姜殷似乎不能理解：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U0kGu8hY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aXgsaqh_">我打起了圆场，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rAvMc-oe">对花魁说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V3s3VfEQ">“哈哈……那个，我带了好些小玩意给你。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HTzWRE37">你看，胭脂、步摇……还有糖人！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="huAO5tmG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sp3_HyUa">花魁姐姐接过东西，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7nu--0eN">笑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A7w_3Bkh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wPC-EuxN">她笑起来真好看。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S57opGoX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wOPBRj-e">姜殷：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nEGtdR2X">“钱绥，我也要糖人！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TtRFBzrM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QE28wO2S">我推开他凑上来的头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kbE4ADKf">“你不能再吃了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hROoOIf8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ys7B1PZj">姜殷：[○･｀Д´･ ○]哼</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wGn7VitF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8FL69ABc">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VwBl86gB">喝酒，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XPhULgW3">听曲儿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i_RZnYHc">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iSdwTyxt">没想到，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JMzmJK61">姜殷这憨憨竟然这么能喝，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="23qqn-Fm">我铆足了劲，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X8JLWltX">也没能把他灌醉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eTaycYsQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dUns8uaU">自己倒有点晕乎乎的了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l0pfAutB">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2x6wM9KY">走之前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IksP_rH-">我醉醺醺地趴在姜殷肩上，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xMq3jDpK">“喝……继续喝……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9TCT9OB2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ohm2iLdE">姜殷摇头：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iXh7EZbZ">“不喝，时辰将近，夜已深。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cqApuNWY">差不多也玩够了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FghtSG8W">你该回去了。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LrjbAXm3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FIq9zMrm">我晃着脑袋，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="usH2Axob">想把里面的酒水晃出来：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ENcJgTPW">“……这样啊……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KZ_G7MLd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JNTs_zq3">印象中，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-KcF9w5K">我是被姜殷扶着回去的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="heZg6HHE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NY163CSt">出厢房门前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8PPZT6uF">花魁姐姐好像对我说了什么，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_owvcaV4">“仲秋……醉花歌舞……望君来……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Eaf-f4dN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZlVz7VNK">我意识迷糊地回了一句，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6ddErJZ8">“明晚加班……”</p>
 <p data-pid="yoZL7xGh">——</p>
 <h2>8月11</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>吃早饭时，</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vgmjZYtp">我注意到，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0WB67_hQ">容玦的衣服越穿越厚了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WrKHGHgg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9tI2zJje">今日中秋，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E24mEnag">春去，夏至，秋来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xC92Nh50">原来已经这么久啦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ke8mhKed">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z-TQh1DC">看着容玦的厚衣服，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vJMhC-oa">感慨。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4ZtKit4i">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EhkLN0WP">季晏突然轻拍了一下桌面，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4HM66i11">瞪我一眼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qAVAkhJr">语气颇为恼怒：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NNWEtWTE">“吃就吃！看什么呀？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7fMw5VVI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pQXuaDtI">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ekfl1Z2Z">又惹你啦？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BnDF9d1f">“你不看我，怎么知道我看啥？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tZwRfdik">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n8zEE_4_">容玦轻笑了一声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hiyg4JPU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pdu-FnPS">季晏气红了脸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="npzGfJ0U">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zuOlpi_o">我：略略略~</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hH1xizJt">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1kBUnFRo">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SppENX3H">白天还是放假的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3OfGroAq">晚上去宫里参加夜宴。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="13D9I13B">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FdVNCvTv">入宫前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iyfDpQUt">容玦帮我添了件衣服，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ga2qi1ih">叮嘱道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WHiiijE4">“勿晚归。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mXH_fOXz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PXLx94Y7">我：“尽量吧。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8J4k1YUX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4XHiOo7p">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fnYsPzv9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MkICV5zx">中秋夜宴前，要先祭月。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5k1kwDUu">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="14mFz84w">胡岩作为钦天监监正，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A4ZJkTha">帮衬着小皇帝主持祭月仪式。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ClSLLTZ_">他穿着一身庄严礼服，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IjOdC4jA">还挺像那么回事的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9jU1Ap1l">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pYgCDPHC">小皇帝在诵读祝文。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y_cCugHz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="p0Uvuogv">“维庚寅仲秋……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5bcKa0oG">普天盛裕，心宇玄黄。重拂仙袂，誓振礼纲。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BuPNqjca">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1fDUJ-vo">竭诚顶礼，感念上苍。敬拜素娥，启佑家邦。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t4DqbLyY">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="winmUNE8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ekLTtYTb">祭月后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fDqThzqM">夜宴开始。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KP7TV63x">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="at37oN36">高官云集，命妇交语。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UnrCbYLX">击鼓奏乐，歌舞升平。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cKuQlh3F">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HySXb7pZ">跳舞的小姐姐好看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3TTBUylS">弹琴的小哥哥好看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n-uswAYj">那个表演杂耍的大叔好逗，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l5Lx5tzg">哈哈哈哈哈哈哈</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Gtqxa_HY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LDALGVrn">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z8K36zQh">夜宴开得差不多，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="okCiPdd9">也该放众官员回家了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rlLhvm2E">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Qz1ErLx_">大家陆陆续续离场。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vqP_VMrw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JlGuEF1r">胡岩跟我道别。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="x4zHZloA">“钱大人，还不走吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MY_aGO5C">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="COdH4LiH">我僵硬地笑了笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wR2pfsOp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SGaQOcLW">QAQ</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e7f7qETC">想起太傅叫我留下来加班。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6PFGTWqD">嘤嘤嘤嘤</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mwMeuP0U">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jdEzgGDE">太傅一步步朝我走来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uEgCJnHX">表面上看，像仙人踏着月色而来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bwdZfpYJ">实际上，是可恶的资本家。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ttVorb-t">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yb4hKWeu">哼!(╯^╰)</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Btu9vUej">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="St2bwS4o">他走近了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7olHyeTP">低头看着坐在案几前的我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Zv8lhDEp">俊目含笑道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AySgb22q">“钱绥，你愿……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QEkbZVY-">同我去城中逛逛吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uOBgVfyz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j8lmPUQf">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uA-YBsMg">不是说加班吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_OYbYvq8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9rK4qJ-y">太傅向我伸出了手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2rR58AKu">他的手很好看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Yi_BMonh">骨肉匀称，苍劲有力。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dR6AA5XM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iXgdG73u">我盯着他的手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fY1srn2Y">满脑子都是，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6VSATe2J">不用加班不用加班不用加班？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3PfDASeT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZS0QbkqN">好耶！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CQbyvTEJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Vm7G9Kc9">我兴奋地站起来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jaD6KZfv">一个脑抽，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HtzAF5nQ">猛拍了一下太傅的手掌。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rVldmGPD">“耶，起来嗨！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_uJ7e1nL">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4Xru8Fbp">太傅手上一痛：…？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="41UJOpyf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vnqNZGzH">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DIVQLJMe">我推着发愣的太傅，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I-5hWU_5">高兴地要去城里玩。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WpKMIfcp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LiIIXcT_">突然，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xz7C0w9Y">腿上一沉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3p9ppita">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nzqw29nw">低头一看，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qndvWiQH">小皇帝不知从哪蹦出来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QGeLqNmn">抱住了我大腿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZCMdDpWz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8DXzR1PI">他眨着卡姿兰大眼睛，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AynG4W5Q">看看太傅，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U0UPkIsk">又看看我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rc-N_p8-">哀求道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="F6DU_4KC">“你们是不是出宫玩？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1aJ0day9">我也要去我也要去——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MPOluNzX">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D4ld3V7v">太傅：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c1iPn1nz">:）保持微笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Yim57D6Z">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cXopOWnS">我犹豫了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9IG9uEVG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DxJBbjoa">小皇帝：猫猫撒娇.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GWGgul1X">“阿宣乖乖的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="unponzFA">不会惹事哦~”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TOe125Y1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jlh-tZw4">行叭，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OFIMpRmX">我薅了一下他的头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OLF9S4dc">微笑道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HhxdqeuK">“你最好是。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fg2IP5in">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tFbw4OmY">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IV9qaJHO">因为是带小皇帝偷渡，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AvHi-BY3">所以要偷偷摸摸地走。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hXyRk8q5">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gNKmsTZD">我抱着小皇帝，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PQp8MJST">快速地从一面墙闪到另一面墙，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a4L14oYF">然后回头向太傅做了个手势，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="97nZlGdm">示意，走！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-qIwBCGV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eX_oezbh">太傅：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gM3Amzvy">看了一眼在一旁巡逻，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6PfEgjJ3">但是装瞎的羽林卫。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0mGzvp20">……汗颜.jpg</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LjsojQmP">你们开心就好。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zHhnGJCG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tbq4_bMB">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Lu-zV-Db">我凭借着神乎其神的步法</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DFlLLeGH">和精妙策略，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uOYcWEpm">躲过了众人的耳目，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OJFJ5gAi">带着太傅和小皇帝来到了皇宫门口。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d01phC-M">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7gGTnzia">门口有守卫。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OFE8PIC9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="R1Q3sTXO">我躲在暗处，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mlzuRE5i">怀里搂着小皇帝，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G4tu_ERT">身后跟着太傅。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c-UwMhTr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V8KeEor0">小皇帝指着一边的高墙，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K2my2Icu">对我说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r2194LQr">“义父，我们是不是要爬墙？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e_Ol-Y4R">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6bho7fqn">我想了想，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hK_H_v4x">郑重地点点头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-DsjT2Iy">“嗯！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fihCO0cV">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VpNLX10F">太傅：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kbvrdckd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gxOO4Zhi">“什么爬墙？我也要！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OC6il26x">一道激动的声音传来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="txm67hGT">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZiWlgal2">我回头，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oiUxrZS5">看到了突然出现的姜殷。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2wKa7zhn">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QoLlGD7K">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JJB1et0t">小皇帝：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0r3ZFrQR">太傅：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ohUuG-0m">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eRykmAUw">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l2afTCIt">四个人一起爬墙。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3bHf_yks">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7q9ckS9Z">我抱着小皇帝，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QUPIHvdg">轻飘飘的从城墙落下。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HkfDqu3r">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lJNOT6tH">姜殷摔了个狗吃屎。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NLtP-1ka">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8a1GsmrK">太傅……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jyzlkqk9">从大门走了出来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TfIxxwWZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eK2qTYhg">奈斯ヾ(◍°∇°◍)ﾉﾞ</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6-XrU9HI">都出来了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bY-4wTLC">去玩！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="73YauU7U">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0e_CZ3tX">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Iiv4Xxb1">没走两步，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Po9kt8Ur">迎面撞上容玦季晏白莲还有小壮。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xKLOCJe_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LGyJnNjj">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="btyvUiCG">“你们怎么在这？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PkEhpLsG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xmNdlq6J">季晏冷眼扫了一下跟在我身后三人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I9_EcBjw">偏头哼了一声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0eRYNqQb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OnU3cGjf">容玦：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="E56eq61S">白莲：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_INtViOs">小壮：“俺们来接你回府！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6BsJ1QaF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eN-FaicV">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2KBm_gwJ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fc8Q7k4R">变成八个人一起去玩。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mW_MjiS0">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="589N8dGC">中秋佳节，圆月当空。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3d68YIqm">夜未深，市内灯火通明、人声嘈杂。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DeIMVGc0">贵家结饰台榭，民间争占酒楼玩月。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WBJFJhQ6">街上有人卖花灯、猜字谜、舞火龙、拜月神……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M2YqSbqR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="paqgzRcp">景很美，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5t_gcVNZ">地方很好玩。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YS62p68l">就是……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rd3qRIPa">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Hu7UH7jK">姜殷扯着我的左手说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bxWiD9Rx">“我们去吃螃蟹！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GVBVYn-Q">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uQzc_sKf">季晏拉着我的右手，喊：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j1PDl8fO">“去猜字谜！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="INHkQZf3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8DSy4pxw">小皇帝抱着我的腿：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CSwRUAY_">“阿宣想放花灯。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lASReHfy">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TU0OVs8Z">“吃螃蟹！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DSU60-t7">“猜字谜！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2RhYZnVd">“放花灯！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XXmlheAV">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rPKHJNvr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KAs6glZ_">容玦&amp;太傅&amp;白莲：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="etR_-IU_">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RXa3YslI">小壮想了想，也凑个热闹：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9re5glZJ">“大人，俺们去赌坊吧！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EjyqKOnK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="90dVAPre">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N9mWnEMY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7VI1SXA9">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yGE567mt">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3SZHt3T5">我看了一圈在场的人，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d9k8LLGq">突然，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qbc6eqYt">灵机一动。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gUEhL7TD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2zu3ovLc">把季晏和容玦的手搭一起，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b3cQedmi">“你们两个去猜字谜。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="moEyPU9G">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c4tSo-N8">把小皇帝推到太傅怀里，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qYIo2T5t">“你们去放花灯。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HhH1VQhx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6OMHsVLJ">把小壮领到白莲面前，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BpA9TZmM">“你们去赌坊。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="j5cT7eFU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z2GMoRMu">完美！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="sZtHlzSz">我真是平平无奇小天才。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nim_NkC2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AMeVnZxU">姜殷很开心：“那你和我去吃螃蟹吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="loQcUZIv">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fayB-MMz">其他人：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UKt60ChO">“不行！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tWOb46I1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eeNjxDP-">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KOTl3Z5H">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uny3VlqU">其实，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Vy9vuJ6n">我本来也没打算去吃东西。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8nQSZ1Qx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q4GuJplN">我出其不意，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kf0eFfHl">使出一个踏雪飞鸿技能，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ijZKzf6d">转身跑了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CGQg0GV4">“玩得开心嘞你们。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="miMYimRZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="plyiluAj">哎，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4OQQUrnh">就是玩儿。</p>
 <p data-pid="jnpEAb2Y">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>8月12</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h3>我来了醉花楼。</h3>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KlnGyclM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ABqMiVw-">没想到吧</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_sKga5P8">哈哈哈哈哈哈哈</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Sf69N27a">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WiMC7Ta2">大笑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gCkT7KxY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N3REVE3T">瞥见熟悉的人影，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="582CmZ0G">笑容消失。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5g8JzzxF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YdF-tnCY">“姜殷，你怎么来了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G9QoUkui">震惊！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bkO2M5ZI">细思恐极，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EYWQeWQP">难道姜殷是个深藏不露的……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tD9pnZaj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yilyEuZK">姜殷：“我来吃螃蟹啊。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1U1FDLGj">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XzDelJBe">我：“我信你个鬼啊！谁来青楼吃螃……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y4ynyZvd">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="67eO2tLm">姜殷指了指立在醉花楼门前的木板，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AaxnimiS">上面赫然写着——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vVf_SkGZ">“仲秋，花雕螃蟹贱售！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eEC0Fu7t">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9C5dQaDy">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1zcW5H66">我错了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UrfPMa63">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_P41WXYD">进醉花楼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5NbaOYjf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YFskx_GL">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wn5wBa0M">我还记着，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kwBbT8Ho">昨晚花魁姐姐邀我来观舞。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vW_Z7V2X">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WTudchGg">今日，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PQ2V9Srv">醉花楼内装饰得很有气氛，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Pz_fgKYc">桂树玉兔金蟾……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-fOYl1AK">颇有蟾宫之意。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uuF0daAr">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3K2Vvj5F">花魁姐姐一身华服，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NQ6zxeuZ">臂弯间绕着窄长的披帛，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CMOa08rY">踏步时丝缕飘动，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5vHyKg8h">有嫦娥之貌。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H1fwsXRZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="18FYEEA2">她在台上翩然起舞。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="weeELG_v">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Anv-3urL">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PNgBL-9I">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eeHD0Ddg">众宾客赞叹不绝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Hv9YXwkU">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y12p4pJV">花魁姐姐顾盼生姿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J-zPIhwH">眉间眼梢风情万种，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o_AulToB">眼神若有若无地落在我这边。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8wkXOXS2">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t7i-eubN">感觉她的眼神充满了期待，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WieXfsOx">我想了想，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ziFt5MR5">决定呐喊助威！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UxaaTfR-">“啊啊啊绝绝子！这样的美貌是真实存在的吗？这是一定是仙子下凡了吧！姐姐，我可以——”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aKkJsDB8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nbMs8400">吵闹的醉花楼突然安静下来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XJNUPiQl">好多人看我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M6VnU2d3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iRifA59-">我：……尴尬。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f0BjOnji">不好意思啊，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KLKQLrhF">忘记你们不兴这个了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1Bu7xZij">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mGuqj8iw">丢人现眼了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4KAjUCsK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kmJhl6YX">灰溜溜地躲厢房里。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zzlW8Qln">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kukBwsHQ">和姜殷一起吃花雕大闸蟹。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HPWET_Ih">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d44JEEor">超好吃！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HFBoTu-I">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="c4mmBH_g">花魁姐姐营业结束，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zCCVEI1S">加入吃螃蟹大军。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fu4qD5qs">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O4xz12ou">吃得只剩一堆壳。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RLPpFfBA">舔嘴唇，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4VMvp_pf">意犹未尽。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ejju8t7M">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xPSf7Utu">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Pn54jBJS">花魁姐姐临时加班，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bDStPncZ">又去跳舞了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ApSwDejM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="js4qpojl">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uLE2mgAO">吃饱喝足，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xim3dLCc">爬上楼顶赏月。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ARnqyhYt">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u5KJ_F-z">我和姜殷并排坐在瓦顶，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qXO7OMo4">看月亮。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cuxh2-UE">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="grWsuuHJ">月亮像月饼，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yTBmOuqG">月饼像月亮。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ANHIbebF">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ho0YRdDf">笑死，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rwR1xKaC">在这还能看到</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="roNOIMFO">在河边放灯的小皇帝和太傅，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gZ3rXBKu">在和字谜摊主争辩的季晏，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EO7uC8il">容玦在吃瓜，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MXUcBZco">小壮拿着糖人追着白莲跑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hxPNK0ff">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tuX1hREE">哈哈哈哈哈哈哈</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="peGZbCFb">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="63-IFUis">“真好啊。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q6OMvnpn">我对姜殷说。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qtsgdCdQ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f5gXvl2o">“嗯。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jie8YY0D">姜殷难得的少话。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0cTv-PKg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nzlzZGbA">夜色渐浓，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6bx8mirM">凉风吹过，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="M5m08ce5">有点冷。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wDwke8ER">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JyEvgNit">姜殷问我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yj_Jkzs9">“你玩得开心吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kSG0uWT3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SAGahtyf">“嗯。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hhw7VgKK">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5IJ9fZ82">“我也开心。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KgaFxYvw">他不看月亮了，转过头来看我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f-LdJQfY">缓缓开口道：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i6iwdu1i">“你还记得吗？之前你问，为什么让胡岩骗你来找我。我说，带我去玩几天我就告诉你……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YYr3rCI7">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zKLXgjcp">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="akphO6Mv">不妙的预感。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lthYtchP">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r0PeE8Cl">于是，我果断说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D3VqDb3B">“不记得！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WLZRc-_P">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vi_qgFpu">姜殷笑了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BRCpzBCJ">他正经地笑起来一点也不像憨憨。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nTb-35a_">朦胧的月光下，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="41npjok_">他白色长发闪着莹润的光泽，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YlQLvx45">真有点像世外高人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LHDIt8vx">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Co3Fx9gj">他看着我笑了好一会儿，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xQGEcUvh">才收敛了上扬的嘴角。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gAh-OwLN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w_cpzstC">我有些不满，问：“你笑什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rXH_in6w">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2ENUtoih">他没有立即回答我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="HxJJCM0C">而是站了起来，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g5Tz_ao8">仰视夜幕，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r7H-vV6M">似乎想离月亮更近一点。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ftoXHMjt">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_z6BGs-Y">姜殷带着凉意的声音传来：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EMSu7faJ">“我笑什么？当然是……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Lvatf7s9">笑你不记得了啦。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1B5KvpNY">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B6gI01h7">他蓦然回首，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GLR9DneU">厉声问我：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5l5pQIOk">“你叫什么？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MgE3Mjul">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hJ68-VvA">我：？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VYZs8CwO">你有毛病啊？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wUsxItbw">“我叫钱……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="a8wJg9zW">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OZykecQx">我突然就止住了声。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hspf0T62">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ME00rNOo">对呀，我……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fpPqOIDU">叫什么？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0OwVGhJ9">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ia_Sft-1">姜殷又笑了，笑得很欠扁。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4TKzTBqi">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EaKfU_Pd">他说：“钱绥，你是钱绥，你也不是钱绥。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9-j9_x3m">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jnhQmqUa">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3b3wIrfh">你搁这搁这呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kdaq54pz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="219EBAqh">姜殷说：“这些日子我玩得很开心，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B4EVjggd">所以……我可以送你回去。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Zn9ergh1">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oDxNbAlw">“回哪？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xs0ow6Qb">“哪来的回哪。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DgMC_Qvm">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UaVZFe4x">我沉默了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IZ_pf51i">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0nkvfe0u">“可是，我不记得了啊。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_8U2tVLq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZNrz-z1t">这次姜殷没有搭话，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nhr7Ch2P">只是漠然地看着我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8ZLDWptf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cIKb9BBT">我这时才注意到，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aQRduhR8">他的瞳色极浅，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hyrEltGS">像玻璃珠子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3mGO9I7O">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UokCRpbS">我问他：“如果我回去了，还能记起来吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1ZD5JIjk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pjX46rZA">这话问得不清不楚的，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PZpSFvut">他却好像听懂了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JIbionKl">姜殷摇了摇头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wdzZQrU8">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VfQKhLnx">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uhi-NFmK">有点生气。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oKeYm6TG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MPutK6UX">我伸手一把扯住他的衣摆，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BnDryxF-">狠狠地往下拽。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QzELaBc3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uDpSboGw">姜殷失去平衡，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wMj4xoaI">重重地跌坐在屋顶。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U2z5vV_D">“？？？你干什么啊？好疼！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2dsJAsYp">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AYS86Iz4">我扯了个鬼脸：略略略——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nYiKOyTG">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bAuc9twh">不想理睬他了，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="CcPPsPcQ">我使出一个飞檐走壁技能，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DbC4HCwu">从屋顶纵身跳下，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wpRGGoBp">只丢下一句话给他。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3J-pZM4z">“不回。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ou9qPdOI">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G76BjjIZ">我足尖轻点落地，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="S085JnQU">去小摊当处买了一盏花灯，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V3JEpjMH">带着它从繁华的市区走到安静的河边，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="AaTKNQaq">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g_klo13U">在河边遇上太傅和小皇帝。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3tp12r4w">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eKOkp0cZ">一起放花灯。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JlzdfQMf">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pR6kADjr">花灯随流水逐渐远去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nNvwpvYZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qAHQ7Pn9">我牵起小皇帝的手，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KxDfQAa3">笑着对太傅说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kKyvup_A">“我们回去吧！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kumUYmmw">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RHDqjulg">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ozSPS8Th">归途中，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SBpzhBz8">熟悉的声音一个个出现。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DA0C2ziA">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ev3c--Po">“钱绥你还知道回来！之前丢下我跑哪去了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6UgzRl9r">“大人，奴家找你找了好久~”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Kwm-Kpil">“所以俺们还去赌坊吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Blw4wopy">“钱绥你怎么扔我一个人在屋顶你知道我怎么下来的吗……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fteb3iNj">“钱绥……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1zxyMLxl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="C7oeQ7CZ">……</p>
 <p data-pid="smSfXJzc"><br>
  完</p>
 <p data-pid="LwkA-QnP">——</p>
 <h2>小番外</h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nORd-v6o">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QMGANtl6">我有点生姜殷的气，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GkM6Q1T_">好多天没理他了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D_6N-rUz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bEKtv8fQ">这个臭猪，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LtvpPI1m">居然在我面前装了这么久大猪蹄子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5vVl10DH">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MP2rTOrq">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aDsSx_MT">深夜加班，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A9sYXetQ">从皇宫出来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="yb5V4WtR">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2X687Kiq">被姜殷拦住。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QpsZf_1w">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_dcN5QZ1">姜殷一副委委屈屈的小媳妇样，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dmQnpLGu">“钱绥，你怎么不来找我玩了？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y5VdDP-3">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I-ggGIFY">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I0f9JpSH">你心里没点数吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XDRB0KO-">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FjHpzEiG">我目不斜视地绕过他继续向前走。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9TVZsGlN">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wV5K3HYw">姜殷跟着我，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7qBqMgI1">叽叽喳喳的像只麻雀。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B1KhVN2U">“哎哎，你不要走嘛……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZWG2aShy">城北新开了一家糕点铺子特别好吃改天我们去尝尝吧……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9KkKmHdo">醉花楼有新来的姑娘哎……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cfAs4wSZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="aXMWh5t1">我：哼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tTKYcHsg">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="g4apkUQ4">……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fPuVsiKk">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="460FxAt2">第二天，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s-zQ9OA-">糕点铺子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ymHlwgpD">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="uGeJOLCS">我咬着绿豆酥，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="78npG6ss">恶狠狠地对姜殷说：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_GW_UAND">“这顿你给钱！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rQ4fHxJo">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MuIHmbQ1">姜殷：！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6S4i9T7c">“可是……我没钱……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zz4xdgXz">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WwA_C6xT">糕点铺子的伙计听见了我们的对话，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dG_iq4Y5">眼睛时不时往这边瞟，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i8oBxEvu">可能是怕我们赖账。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lz8H7EaC">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PJIIFt1j">我：……</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IislljVh">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G0oOtm-b">最后，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_naJCRLM">还是我掏钱。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OIFBElJZ">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4wfToOeO">走了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bXUo708M">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="X1YeHtrF">“钱绥你走这么快干什么呀，等等我嘛……”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PZJM7ncl">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hRokpDcI">姜殷绝对是个铁憨憨，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZS8k77xn">一点眼力见都没有，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H2MiBIAd">没看见我头上都冒火了吗？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xDJfDE_G">还要赶着上趟惹我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9enHHAmM">——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="93l7Vpmn">我突然停住脚步，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mPcLcvsw">友善地对姜殷微笑。</p>
